# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

A Dremora warrior wielding a steel war axe

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

A Dremora warlock wielding fire

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons
- ***[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*** — The story of a youth summoning a Dremora
- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora

# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

- ***[Spirit of the Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_the_Daedra "Skyrim:Spirit of the Daedra")*** — A look into the Daedric mindset
- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons
- ***[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*** — The story of a youth summoning a Dremora
- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora

# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

A Dremora warrior wielding a steel war axe

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons

- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora

# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

A Dremora warrior wielding a steel war axe

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

- ***[Spirit of the Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_the_Daedra "Skyrim:Spirit of the Daedra")*** — A look into the Daedric mindset
- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons
- ***[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*** — The story of a youth summoning a Dremora
- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora

# Skyrim:Dremora

## Overview

Dremora at the Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon

**Dremora** are humanoid [Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"). They are often very intelligent and are generally hostile. In [lore](/wiki/Lore:Dremora "Lore:Dremora"), it is said they can be found in clans of large numbers in the wastes of [Oblivion](/wiki/Lore:Oblivion "Lore:Oblivion"). Dremora are grouped into several different castes: Churl, Caitiff, Kynval, Kynreeve, Kynmarcher, Markynaz, and Valkynaz. Dremora are a rare sight in Skyrim, only appearing as summoned creatures and in a few set locations, such as the [Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Mehrunes_Dagon "Skyrim:Shrine of Mehrunes Dagon"), [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze"), [Azura's Star Interior](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura%27s_Star_Interior "Skyrim:Azura's Star Interior"), and the [Deadlands](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadlands "Skyrim:Deadlands")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cause "Skyrim:The Cause").

The other way to encounter Dremora in Skyrim is by summoning one. There are a few ways to summon Dremora:

- The [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"), a reward from the quest [A Night To Remember](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Night_To_Remember "Skyrim:A Night To Remember"), will summon a leveled melee fighter Dremora for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") spell [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord") will summon a [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) for 60 seconds, or 120 seconds with the appropriate Conjuration perks.
- The [Atronach Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge "Skyrim:Atronach Forge") can be used to summon hostile Dremora, which will obviously attack anybody or anything on sight.
- The [Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell") quest involves summoning an [Unbound Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound_Dremora "Skyrim:Unbound Dremora"); this Dremora cannot be summoned anywhere other than the roof of the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"). Once again, this will be automatically hostile to everything it encounters.
- The [Wabbajack](/wiki/Skyrim:Wabbajack "Skyrim:Wabbajack") has a chance to momentarily turn the target into a hostile Dremora.

## Dremora Types

There are three types of Dremora, based on their preferred fighting style: melee fighters, archers, and warlocks. All Dremora are [NPCs](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") with [black souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls"). All types of Dremora always drop a [Daedra Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra_Heart "Skyrim:Daedra Heart") on death; they're one of the few guaranteed sources of this rare ingredient.

### Melee Fighters

These Dremora belong to the [Dremora](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_(class) "Skyrim:Dremora (class)") NPC [class](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes "Skyrim:Classes") and use one or two-handed weapons in battle. They wear a [unique version](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear") of [Daedric Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Armor "Skyrim:Daedric Armor") available only to Dremora and wield a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), or [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), all of which are enchanted with [fire damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage"). The type of enchantment depends on the quality of the material, as follows:

- **[Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") or [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel "Skyrim:Steel"):** [of Embers](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Embers "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Burning](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Burning "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of Scorching](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Scorching "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite"):** of Scorching, [of Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_Fire "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons"), [of the Blaze](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Blaze "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") or [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, [of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons")

They also carry an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and will drop a Daedra Heart on death.

A Dremora warrior wielding a steel war axe

[^1](#note_DremoraLord)This Dremora is also the template used for the [Dremora Lord](#Dremora_Lord) summoned with Conjure Dremora Lord.

### Archers

These Dremora have the [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") NPC class and wield fire-enchanted bows to fight from a distance. They wear the same unique Daedric Armor as their melee counterparts and use one of the following enchanted bows:

- **[Hunting Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"):** of Embers, of Burning, of Scorching
- **[Glass Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Bow "Skyrim:Glass Bow"):** of Scorching, of Fire, of the Blaze
- **[Ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Bow "Skyrim:Ebony Bow") or [Daedric Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric"):** of Fire, of the Blaze, of the Inferno

They also carry an iron dagger, one iron arrow, and a quiver of up to 20 [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Arrow "Skyrim:Orcish Arrow"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow"), or [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), depending on their level.

### Warlocks

Dremora warlocks are members of the [Destruction Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction "Skyrim:CombatMageDestruction") NPC class and prefer to use spells in combat. They wear unique [black robes and boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Dremora_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear"). In case they are forced into melee combat, they carry an iron dagger and a mace, sword, war axe, warhammer, greatsword, or battleaxe (any quality from iron to elven).

### Summonable Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord

A Dremora Lord can be summoned using either [Conjure Dremora Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Dremora_Lord "Skyrim:Conjure Dremora Lord"), an Expert level Conjuration spell or the [Sanguine Rose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine_Rose "Skyrim:Sanguine Rose"). The Dremora Lord is a Dremora Valynaz, a melee fighter equipped with the standard unique Daedric armor that wields a [Daedric Greatsword of the Inferno](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons#of_the_Inferno "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons").

The Dremora Lord has 545 health and 230 stamina. [Dragon Priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead#Dragon_Priests "Skyrim:Undead") cannot take control of conjured Dremora Lords. Furthermore, while the Dremora Lord is technically not an [Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedra "Skyrim:Daedra"), it is affected by the [Summoner](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoner "Skyrim:Summoner") and [Atromancy](/wiki/Skyrim:Atromancy "Skyrim:Atromancy") Conjuration perks, although it is **not** affected by [Elemental Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Elemental_Potency "Skyrim:Elemental Potency"). The [Twin Souls](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Souls "Skyrim:Twin Souls") perk also applies to Dremora Lords, making it possible to have both a Dremora Lord and an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") or [thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thrall "Skyrim:Thrall"), or two Dremora Lords. Unlike other NPC Dremoras, Dremora Lords cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") for weapons or armor, and they will not drop Daedra Hearts because their bodies disappear upon death. They are also immune to [all Soul Trap effects](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)").

#### Dremora Lord Dialogue

| In combat | After defeating an enemy | After spotting an enemy | After losing sight of an enemy | After being defeated |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - *"I will feast on your heart."* - *"I honor my lord by destroying you!"* - *"You are weak, mortal."* - *"Are you prepared for your death?"* - *"Oblivion take you!"* - *"You will bleed!"* - *"Fall before me!"* | - *"No match at all."* - *"There could be no other end."* | - *"I smell weakness..."* - *"A challenger is near..."* - *"Another who seeks death."* - *"There you are weakling!"* - *"You meet your end, mortal."* - *"No one escapes!"* - *"Now you suffer!"* - *"You return, foolish mortal?"* | - *"Hiding will not save you now."* - *"You cannot escape me!"* - *"Quiet again."* - *"Nothing after all."* | - *"No... not by a mortal..."* - *"It cannot... end like this..."* |

## Notes

- In the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), you can see that the Dremora race uses the [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") race as a base, with the only changes being: horns, their own unique skin tone (dark with red facial markings), unique eyes, and their in-game height being equal to that of the [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf").
- Although there is an Archer class for Dremora, they do not appear in the game; only the melee fighters and mages can be encountered.
- The Daedric Prince [Sanguine](/wiki/Skyrim:Sanguine "Skyrim:Sanguine") appears in the form of a Dremora.
- Several human NPCs are [classified](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Dremora_Class "Category:Skyrim-Dremora Class") in the game data as Dremora, due to that class being used as a default value.
- Seven of the Dremora dialogue lines appear in the book *[I Was Summoned by a Mortal](/wiki/Online:I_was_Summoned_by_a_Mortal "Online:I was Summoned by a Mortal")* in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- The aforementioned Archer Dremora were given Nord voices rather than the voices given to Melee and Warlock Dremora. **?**
- Dremora may not voice their death quotes when they die; only pained grunts or yells are heard, instead.
- Reanimated Dremora may equip invisible items in their hands if they were placed on the corpse before reanimation took place.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

### Books

- ***[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*** — A description of various Daedra
- ***[Spirit of the Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_the_Daedra "Skyrim:Spirit of the Daedra")*** — A look into the Daedric mindset
- ***[There Be Dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:There_Be_Dragons "Skyrim:There Be Dragons")*** by [Torhal Bjorik](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Torhal_Bjorik "Lore:Books by Author") — A report on the nature of dragons
- ***[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*** — The story of a youth summoning a Dremora
- ***[Varieties of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Varieties_of_Daedra "Skyrim:Varieties of Daedra")*** by [Aranea Drethan](/wiki/Lore:Books_by_Author#Aranea_Drethan "Lore:Books by Author") — An analysis of Daedra forms, focusing primarily on the Dremora

Drennen's ghost

**Drennen** is the [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") of a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") who met his death in [Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel"). He now wanders the halls of his tomb with his similarly ghostly companions [Breya](/wiki/Skyrim:Breya "Skyrim:Breya"), [Watches-The-Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots "Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots"), and [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms").

His corpse can be found in [Avanchnzel Animoncultory](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel_Animoncultory "Skyrim:Avanchnzel Animoncultory") in a sloping corridor after the factory-like room. On his body is his [studded armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Studded_Armor "Skyrim:Studded Armor") and a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), as well as an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

### Unfathomable Depths

As you first enter Avanchnzel you will see the ghost of Drennen speaking to the other ghosts:

:   **Drennen**: *"I don't like this place. It feels like we're being... watched."*
:   **Breya**: *"It's a simple job, Drennen. We get in, we steal the Lexicon, we leave. Don't get jumpy."*
:   **Fathoms**: *"If you two cannot handle this, we can find others to hire."*
:   **Roots**: *"Enough. Their services will be more than adequate. Let us continue."*

Further in the ruins you will see him having a conversation with Watches-The-Roots:

:   **Drennen**: *"This place is unbelievable."*
:   **Roots**: *"Indeed. Avanchnzel is as much a library as it is a city. Built to hold the vast memories of the Dwemer."*

In Avanchnzel Animoncultory at the campsite:

:   **Drennen**: *"This place is huge."*
:   **Roots**: *"It is large, indeed. I did not anticipate Avanchnzel's size or the time needed to uncover the entrance. A few hours sleep and we should be ready to continue through."*
:   **Drennen**: *"Maybe we should turn back. I don't want to sleep here."*
:   **Roots**: *"Drennen, you do understand that the Lexicon at the bottom of this place holds the accumulated memories of centuries of Dwemer."*
:   **Breya**: *"Not to mention our pay."*
:   **Drennen**: *"So?"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"So we're not turning back, you fool."*
:   **Breya**: *"Besides, you're not afraid of a few sleeping metal men. Are you, Drennen?"*

Just before the doors to the Avanchnzel Boilery:

:   **Drennen**: *"I can't do this. We shouldn't be here. I'm sorry."*
:   **Breya**: *"Drennen!"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"Let the field mouse run. Your pay will be double."*
:   **Breya**: *"My pay will be nothing if we die in here!"*
:   **Roots**: *"Calm yourself, Breya. We are closing in on the Lexicon. I can feel it calling. We'll continue without Drennen."*

## Notes

- Unused scripting in the quest would've given every member of the party a full set of Dwarven armor, although this never happens, and it's unknown what purpose this would've served.

## Bugs

- A scene near the giant Dwemer factory may be missing, since the trigger for it is located outside of the map. **?**

:   **Fathoms**: *"The Lexicon had better be worth all this trouble."*
:   **Roots**: *"I assure you, it is. The knowledge contained in the Lexicon created everything you see around you. Properly controlled, it has knowledge enough to turn paupers into kings."*
:   **Drennen**: *"You sure that's power we're meant to have?"*
:   **Roots**: *"Absolutely."*

| Buys | Spells ([Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), [Clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"), [Daedric Artifacts](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Artifacts "Skyrim:Daedric Artifacts"), [Jewelry](/wiki/Skyrim:Jewelry "Skyrim:Jewelry"), [Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls"), [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [Staves](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves")) | | |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50+(PC-1)×8.3 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50+(PC-1)×5 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50+(PC-1)×1.7 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, **[Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion")**, [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") | | |

| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions_C#College_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Factions C") (Wizard); [CrimeFactionWinterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionWinterhold "Skyrim:CrimeFactionWinterhold"); [Drevis Neloren Services](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren_Services "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren Services"); [Illusion Trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Trainer "Skyrim:Illusion Trainer"); [Skill Trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Trainer "Skyrim:Skill Trainer") | | |

Drevis Neloren in the Arcanaeum

**Drevis Neloren** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [sorcerer](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerIllusionMaster "Skyrim:TrainerIllusionMaster") and an instructor at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). He is the master [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") for [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion"), able to train you to level 90. After you officially become part of the College, he will ask you to don some [magical gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystic_Tuning_Gloves "Skyrim:Mystic Tuning Gloves") for a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Out_of_Balance "Skyrim:Out of Balance") where you have to cleanse various magicka focus points around the college. He will also give a [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell") for the master Illusion spells, and will sell many [Illusion spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Spells "Skyrim:Illusion Spells").

Drevis wears [master robes of illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Robes_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Master Robes of Illusion") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing"), and carries an unenchanted [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

He can be found during most days in his room on the lower floor of the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"), waking at 7am to eat, drink, and perform alchemy for most of the day with the exception of between 10am to 3pm, during which time he will be found in the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). He will then go to sleep at 11pm.

## Related Quests

- **[Illusion Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell")**: Find some books about [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") magic to further your Illusion skills.
- **[Out of Balance](/wiki/Skyrim:Out_of_Balance "Skyrim:Out of Balance")**: Purify the focus points for magical energy around the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").

## Dialogue

Upon first meeting Drevis, he will be surprised that you are talking to him, and say:

:   *"You... You can see me?"*

:   :   **I... No, I can't see you. Not at all.**
    :   *"But you can hear me, obviously. Something still isn't quite right. At least I'm making progress."*

:   :   **Of course I can.**
    :   *"Confound it all. I was quite sure I was invisible, or at least transparent."*

Either leads to:

:   **Which are the best Illusion spells?**
:   *"Oh my, that's quite a difficult question. Never underestimate the ability to influence others. Whether they're friends or foes, they're almost all susceptible to Illusion spells. They can turn the tide of a battle in a moment's notice. There are also spells that help in avoiding conflict altogether. Invisibility is tricky to master, but exceptionally useful."*

Upon finishing a conversation with Drevis:

:   *"If only I could be free of the mundane, day-to-day activities life so often requires."*
:   *"Illusion really is the least appreciated of the schools of magic."*
:   *"You know, they say knowledge is its own reward."*

### Conversations

While inside the Arcanaeum, he will have conversations with other College members, such as [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub"):

**Urag:** *"Are you looking for any specific volumes, Drevis?"*
**Drevis:** *"Hmm? Oh, no. No, not really. I... Actually, I've forgotten what I was looking for."*
**Urag:** *"Ah. Well, then. Let me know if you need anything."*
**Drevis:** *"What's that? Oh yes, yes. Thank you, I will."*

He will also react negatively to [Colette Marence](/wiki/Skyrim:Colette_Marence "Skyrim:Colette Marence") if she approaches him:

**Colette:** *"How are you, Drevis?"*
**Drevis:** *"Ugh. What do you want?"*
**Colette:** *"Why should I want anything? Why can't I simply be sociable with my colleagues?"*
**Drevis:** *"I'm busy right now, Colette."*
**Colette:** *"Well, then. Fine. Have a nice day."*

## Lecture: The Doomstones

Drevis holding a lecture

Drevis will hold lectures in the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") occasionally, in which he will be heard saying the following:

*"The existence of so-called 'Doomstones' throughout Skyrim has been repeatedly verified. The meaning of these stones has not. The prevailing opinion of Skyrim natives is that the stones are indeed magical in nature. While there is no direct evidence of this, it does seem likely. References to similar stones appear in lore throughout the various Tamrielic cultures. None, however, exactly match the markings or distribution of Skyrim's stones. At present, there is no confirmation of any of the various theories surrounding the nature of these stones. Their relative positions do not indicate that any individual stone is part of a larger, unobserved pattern. Also, their placement throughout Skyrim does not correspond to any known magical phenomenon. The age of the stones themselves has yet to be officially determined. It has been widely assumed that they were placed during the Merethic Era. Writings from that period, including those of Ysgramor himself, do not mention the stones and thus this idea cannot be verified. Nonetheless, many are drawn to these stones based on the local stories describing them as a source of significant power. The College will continue to research these intriguing objects, and of course any findings will be relayed with all possible haste."*

### Main Quest

During the quest [Containment](/wiki/Skyrim:Containment "Skyrim:Containment"), when Drevis learns that there are [magic anomalies](/wiki/Skyrim:Magic_Anomaly "Skyrim:Magic Anomaly") attacking Winterhold, he will say to himself: *"I hope this isn't something I did."* After the quest, he will occasionally say in passing: *"Have you seen Mirabelle around? I know she's dead, but I thought... Well, I thought she might stop in and say hello anyway."*

After you defeat Ancano and the Eye of Magnus is removed from the College, Drevis can be heard saying: *"The Eye of Magnus. Here, but lost. Slipped through our grasp. Oh, what we might have learned."* as well as: *"I wonder what we could've done with the Eye, had it been put to better use?"*

Once you have become the Arch-Mage of the College, Drevis will occasionally say: *"We have survived difficult times, and are better mages for it. We owe you that, Arch-Mage. Thank you."*

### Out of Balance

*"I'm busy right now, Colette."*

After becoming officially inducted into the College of Winterhold, you can ask Drevis if there is anything [he needs help with](/wiki/Skyrim:Out_of_Balance "Skyrim:Out of Balance"):

:   **Is there any College business I can assist with?**
:   *"There may be a matter in which your... skills... could be useful. The various points of focus for magic energies around the College have become polluted, and need cleansing."*
:   **Why do these "energies" need to be cleansed?**
:   *"As you may be aware, the College has gone to great lengths to purify and enhance the natural energies of the world. This both enhances our connection to the realm of magic, and eliminates possible interference from outside sources. These energies, on occasion, become... polluted. Effort must be made to see that they are kept pure, clean. Do you wish to aid in this cleansing?"*

:   :   **All right, I'll help.**
    :   *"Very well. These specially enchanted gloves will allow you to delve directly into the focal points for these energies. Go to each focal point and remove whatever impurities you may find there. Return the gloves to me when you have finished. Please exercise caution. This is not a procedure without possible... consequences."*

:   :   **Maybe some other time.**
    :   *"I see."*

If you agree to help, Drevis will hand you a pair of [mystic tuning gloves](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystic_Tuning_Gloves "Skyrim:Mystic Tuning Gloves").

Returning to him without finishing the task and asking for clarification:

:   **What did you need me to do?**
:   *"Use the gloves to clear the focal points. Return to me when you have finished. I thought I made this rather clear."*

Successfully cleansing all of the focal points and returning to Drevis to report that the focal points have been cleansed:

:   **Your focal points have been, uh, cleansed.**
:   *"Yes, they have. I can feel the difference already. But of course, I'm far more in tune with these sorts of things than most. Thank you. I appreciate your assistance."*

### The Black Star

During the quest [The Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star"), you can ask Drevis if he knows anything about the study of stars. He will say:

:   **Is there an elven mage here that studies stars?**
:   *"I know plenty of spells that produce light, but stars? Hmm. There was that problem a few years ago, but that couldn't be related."*

:   :   **Something tells me that it is.**
    :   *"You should go into town and talk to an elf named Nelacar. He was involved in the whole mess."*

:   :   **What is it? What happened?**
    :   *"There was some bother about a group of mages being exiled. I can't remember what the details were. I think one of them came back. Nelacar. Stays at the Frozen Hearth, but I don't know why. He's not welcome in the College."*

### Master Illusionist

Once you reach level 100 (see [bugs](#Bugs)) in [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion"), you can ask Drevis if there is anything [more to be learned](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell") about Illusion magic:

:   **What else is there to be learned about Illusion Magic?**
:   *"You have gone beyond my teachings, which is quite a feat. I did not think it possible. But there is always more to learn. I believe you are ready for the next step."*
:   **What's the next step?**
:   *"Knowledge of truly powerful Illusion spells is here at the College, but it is hidden from those who might misuse it. I shall teach you a spell to discern things hidden from others. With it, you will be able to acquire the texts you need. Bring all four to me, and I shall use them to inscribe the spells for you."*

Upon acquiring all of the books and telling Drevis that you have them all:

:   **Here are the texts you requested.**
:   *"Yes, very good. Here, then, is the first of the Illusion spells you sought."*

Drevis knows the following spells:

[Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")
:   [Ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironflesh "Skyrim:Ironflesh")

[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")

## Notes

- Despite being the master trainer in Illusion, Drevis does not know any Illusion spells.
- Drevis Neloren also appears in the [Heroes of Skyrim](/wiki/Legends:Heroes_of_Skyrim "Legends:Heroes of Skyrim") card expansion for *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*, as the card [Winterhold Illusionist](/wiki/Legends:Winterhold_Illusionist "Legends:Winterhold Illusionist").

## Bugs

- Drevis Neloren's opening dialogue for the [Illusion Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell") requires a skill level of 100 despite the quest only requiring a skill level of 90.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
