Dreyla Alor

**Dreyla Alor** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") living in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), although she hates [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim"), as her time is spent trying to eke out a living at her shop. She wants to return to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), but doesn't want to leave her widowed father, [Fethis](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor"). Her mother died during an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") raid, along with nearly everyone else in their town, as they lived only a league from the border with [Black Marsh](/wiki/Lore:Black_Marsh "Lore:Black Marsh"). She is in a relationship with [Captain Veleth](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Veleth "Skyrim:Captain Veleth"), but must visit him secretly because her father does not approve.

Dreyla wears a [Dunmer outfit](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Outfit "Skyrim:Dunmer Outfit") with [Dunmer shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_Shoes "Skyrim:Dunmer Shoes"), and she carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Alor_House_Key "Skyrim:Alor House Key") to her house, and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

She gets up at 6am to have a two-hour breakfast with her father. At 8am she leaves the house and goes over to The Retching Netch to drink for two hours, together with her lover, Captain Modyn Veleth. Once she gets done drinking, she decides to go browsing at the marketplace for 7 full hours before returning to drinking at the Netch for 4 more hours. Afterwards, she returns to her house to wander around some more and at midnight, she either heads to the [Earth Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Earth_Stone "Skyrim:Earth Stone"), to work for six hours, or if the stone has been [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), she heads to bed.

## Related Quests

- **[It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste")**: Distribute [Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri")'s [Sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma") to the citizens of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

## Dialogue

Her greetings can be:

:   *"Miserable... just miserable. I hate this place."*
:   *"This island's nothing but a pile of rubble. What's the point trying to make a life here?"*
:   *"You stuck in Raven Rock too? Horrible isn't it."*
:   *"If you're looking to purchase something, speak to my father, Fethis."*

Once she's free from [Miraak's](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") control:

:   *"I can't believe that I was building that shrine at night... I never knew."*

If she is located at the Earth Stone when it is cleansed:

:   *"I know you risked a lot freeing me from Miraak's control. Thank you!"*
:   *"What if Miraak decides to make us do something else next... like kill someone we love. I can't bear the thought!"*

If you've helped Raven Rock get [back](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent") [on its](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead") [feet](/wiki/Skyrim:Served_Cold "Skyrim:Served Cold"), she'll be very grateful:

:   *"The mines are open and the shop is busy again. Thank you!"*

If spoken to:

:   **You don't like it on Solstheim?**
:   *"Don't like it? I hate it! Every day it's the same thing. We open the shop, we hardly sell a thing, we close the shop and go to sleep. What kind of a life is that?"*
:   **Why not return to Morrowind?**
:   *"Oh, believe me... I'd be on the first ship off of this miserable island if I could. But I'm not sure I could do that to my father. I think it would break his heart. We've already lost my mother, I don't want to leave him alone."*
:   **How did your mother die?**
:   *"We lived in a settlement perhaps a league from the border of Black Marsh, the homeland of the Argonians. Even though the Argonian Invasion ended a long time ago, there are still a few scale-skin clans that live within our borders. To put it simply, they attacked our settlement and slaughtered almost everyone. It was horrible."*

When exiting conversation:

:   *"Keep yourself safe... Solstheim's still a dangerous place."*

### Dragonborn

:   **What's being built outside of town?**
:   *"There's a shrine there, but I'm not sure what it means..."*
:   **Can you tell me more about the shrine near town?**
:   *"Why can't I remember? I was sure it was important."*

:   **Do you know someone called Miraak?**
:   *"I think so, but I'm not sure where I heard the name."*
:   **Is there anything you can tell me?**
:   *"I don't know why, but I'm thinking about a temple, here on the island. Maybe it was just a bad dream."*

### It's All In The Taste

When asked if she [wants a drink](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste") from [Geldis](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri"), she'll gladly accept:

:   **Geldis Sadri wants you to try his new drink.**
:   *"At least my father will let me drink whatever I want without complaining. Tell Geldis I appreciate it."*

### Reluctant Steward

If you ask her if she wants to be [Neloth's](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward"), she'll immediately decline

:   **Do you want to be the new steward of Tel Mithryn?**
:   *"My father needs me. He can't run his market stand alone. Besides, Neloth is as loony as a skooma addict. He wanted my father to import a white mammoth. Alive!"*
:   **Know anyone that might take the job?**
:   *"You could try [Drovas Relvi](/wiki/Skyrim:Drovas_Relvi "Skyrim:Drovas Relvi"). He came in here asking my father if he needed any odd jobs done. Seemed kind of desperate."*

## Conversations

She can often be seen talking with either her father, Geldis Sadri or Captain Modyn Veleth, her lover.

**Fethis**: *"I never got a chance to thank you for everything you've done. Ever since your mother died..."*
**Dreyla**: *"You don't need to say anything, father. I miss her too."*
**Fethis**: *"Had we only left a day earlier... she'd still be with us. It's my fault she's dead."*
**Dreyla**: *"It was her time, father. None of us have any control over that. You mustn't blame yourself."*

**Fethis**: *"Dreyla! I told you I didn't want you seeing him anymore. Must I lock you into the house at night?"*
**Dreyla**: *"Father, Captain Veleth and I are in love. He means everything to me. Am I to simply ignore my own heart?"*
**Fethis**: *"He's twice your age and only wants to marry into our family to use my contacts at the East Empire Company. No, I won't allow it."*
**Dreyla**: *"Your precious "contacts" have yet to conjure up a scrap of food or work for us, father. Don't make me choose, father... I beg you!"*

**Geldis**: *"Dreyla, I have a message for you."*
**Dreyla**: *"Tell my father if he wants to speak to me, he should do it in person."*
**Geldis**: *"It's not from your father. It's from Captain Veleth."*
**Dreyla**: *"Oh my goodness, I'm so sorry, Geldis! Please, tell me... what did he say?"*
**Geldis**: *"He said he'll meet you where you met for the first time. He said you'd know what it means."*
**Dreyla**: *"I do! Thank you."*

**Dreyla**: *"I don't know if I can do this anymore, Modyn."*
**Modyn**: *"Is it because of your father? Or is it me?"*
**Dreyla**: *"He's never been the same since my mother died. I don't think he ever wants me to feel the pain he suffers."*
**Modyn**: *"At some point, you're going to have to choose. No matter the outcome, I'll always respect your decision."*

## Bugs

- She is incorrectly referred to as 'Dinya' in the note *[Dearest Dinya](/wiki/Skyrim:Dearest_Dinya "Skyrim:Dearest Dinya")* which was written by her lover, Modyn Veleth.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- Despite it being clear in-game that she is the daughter of Fethis, the game data incorrectly has them set up as husband and wife.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Drifa

## Overview

| Drifa (RefID: 00019DCF) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | | |

Drifa

**Drifa** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker") living in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). She owns the [Pawned Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn") with her husband [Bersi Honey-Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Bersi_Honey-Hand "Skyrim:Bersi Honey-Hand"), and will take over the business if anything happens to him. She cares deeply for him but thinks that he spends too much time worrying about crime and corruption in Riften and not enough about himself. He believes that someone is trying to make a move to take the Pawned Prawn from them, but she thinks he is just being paranoid.

Drifa wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#000f8715 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#000cee82 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"). She is equipped with a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") which can be up to [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven "Skyrim:Elven") quality, and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn_Key "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn Key") to her store, as well as a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

## Dialogue

Drifa greets visitors to the Pawned Prawn with:

:   *"Hello. Welcome to the Pawned Prawn."*
:   *"If there's anything you need, I'd be glad to help you."*

Her normal greetings:

:   *"My husband Bersi will be the death of me. He spends too much time worrying about Riften and not enough about himself."*
:   *"All the crime and corruption in Riften is really getting to him... and now that we hear rumors about the dragons, he's been very depressed."*
:   *"Bersi's afraid that someone's making a move to take the Pawned Prawn from us. I think he's being paranoid."*
:   *"We both own the Pawned Prawn together, but he's singlehandedly kept the place running despite all our problems."*
:   *"I just care about my husband so much and I hate to see him in this state."*

She will say goodbye with

:   *"Be careful out there... Riften can be dangerous."*

### Spread the Love

During the quest [Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love"), you have the option to give her a [missive](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara"), which she will accept gratefully with:

:   *"Oh, how kind! Thank you."*

### Taking Care of Business

During the quest [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business"), you have the option of persuading Bersi Honey-Hand to repay his debt with the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") by breaking his prized Dwarven urn. While you are breaking it and Bersi is lamenting his ill fortune, Drifa will loudly tell her husband to

:   *"Just pay them, Bersi!"*

## Conversations

Drifa may also be seen having random conversations with her husband Bersi or other Riften residents:

:   **Bersi**: *"Drifa? I was looking through our books and there's an entry for 'spices.' Says we spent 300 septims. What is that?"*
:   **Drifa**: *"Spices? I'm certain I have no idea what you're talking about."*
:   **Bersi**: *"You sure? It was in your handwriting. If you can't keep the books straight then let me do them."*
:   **Drifa**: *"Oh, yes... spices. That was a special order for someone in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). Should be along any day now. Don't let it worry you, my dear."*

:   **Drifa**: *"We got a few pieces of jewelry at the [Prawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawned_Prawn "Skyrim:Pawned Prawn"), Madesi. Want to come take a look at them later?"*
:   **[Madesi](/wiki/Skyrim:Madesi "Skyrim:Madesi")**: *"I wish I could, milady. Sadly, I haven't sold enough of my own jewelry let alone buy some from you. I'm sorry."*
:   **Drifa**: *"Oh, I'm so sorry. I'm certain Bolli*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *would be happy to lend you a few septims."*
:   **Madesi**: *"Much appreciated, Lady Drifa, but I'll manage."*

:   **Drifa**: *"[Mjoll](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness")! I'm glad I found you."*
:   **Mjoll**: *"What is it, Drifa? What's the matter?"*
:   **Drifa**: *"It's Bersi. He's getting so angry about the corruption in Riften, he said he's going to walk right up to [Maven](/wiki/Skyrim:Maven_Black-Briar "Skyrim:Maven Black-Briar") and give her a piece of his mind."*
:   **Mjoll**: *"If I see him, I'll make sure he doesn't do anything brash. Don't worry."*

She may be accosted by either [Snilf](/wiki/Skyrim:Snilf "Skyrim:Snilf") or [Edda](/wiki/Skyrim:Edda "Skyrim:Edda"), Riften's two beggars. Either way, she will take pity on them, telling Snilf, *"Very well, please use it for food."* and Edda, *"Oh, very well. Just try and clean yourself up."*

## Notes

- Drifa uses Pawned Prawn greetings even when she's not manning the store if Bersi is dead.
- Several lines of dialogue incorrectly refer to Drifa as being married to [Bolli](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolli "Skyrim:Bolli").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The audio and dialogue text correctly refer to [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor") instead.
- A [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Ceremony "Skyrim:Argonian Ceremony") addressed to Drifa from [Talen-Jei](/wiki/Skyrim:Talen-Jei "Skyrim:Talen-Jei") asking about an Argonian wedding ceremony in [the temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") appears next to [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu")'s bed in the temple. However, Drifa has no connection with the temple. Given where the letter is found, it's likely Dinya Balu was meant to be the recipient instead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, addresses this issue. The letter is addressed to Dinya instead.

## Bugs

- Drifa doesn't sleep as she was intended to.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- Drifa isn't marked as essential prior to [A Chance Arrangement](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement"), and if she is killed before completing the quest then the succeeding quest, [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business"), will not start.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- After Taking Care of Business, Drifa may have a conversation with [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei") in the plaza where she indicates that Bolli was involved rather than her husband: *"One of them came in and demanded payment. Bolli tried to tell them no; stood up to them, but..."*
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- During the quest [Caught Red Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_Red_Handed "Skyrim:Caught Red Handed") Bolli will remark he never slept with any woman other than his wife Drifa; however, Bolli is actually married to [Nivenor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nivenor "Skyrim:Nivenor").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge

## Overview

Driftshade Refuge

**Driftshade Refuge** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"). It contains two zones: *[Driftshade Refuge](#Driftshade_Refuge)* and *[Driftshade Cellar](#Driftshade_Cellar)*.

The dilapidated fort, almost lost beneath snowdrifts, is now a base of command for the Silver Hand. Its remote location in the mountains and apparent disappearance from local memory are ideal for concealing activities. It was once a much larger fort, as seen by the broken walls a short distance from the only remaining intact building.

## Related Quests

- **[Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge")**: Retrieve the Fragments of Wuuthrad and wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are two Silver Hands on guard duty outside the fort. One has lookout duty atop the main building, while the other stands guard by the door. They will warn you against approaching the fort, and turn hostile if you choose to venture too close. To get to the archer on top of the building, you will need to go around the back, where a wooden ramp is located. There are a total of twenty-one snowberry bushes along the path leading up to the front entrance, with two more off to the left of the building, and two more near the cart around the back.

### Driftshade Refuge

The kitchen

After following the stairs down from the entrance, you will come to a multi-junction room. There are two Silver Hands patrolling the middle corridor, which leads to a door that is held shut by a wooden bar on the other side. The eastern corridor has collapsed, so the only option is the western room. Before looting, you may wish to dispose of the Silver Hand in the adjoining room to the right. The first room holds only a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") on the table, and an apothecary's satchel on the top shelf of the second set of shelves from the right. The table to the right in the second room holds a few iron shields and an iron weapon, and a set of shelves to the left holds an assortment of iron weapons. The table to the far left holds a filled random soul gem and a random healing potion.

The next corridor leads to a large two-leveled room. Two more Silver Hands patrol here, one on the top level to the left, and the other straight ahead on the lower level. On the upper level there are several sets of shelves mostly holding [ruined](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and [burned books](/wiki/Skyrim:Burned_Book "Skyrim:Burned Book"), however among these are several common books, a random potion of stamina and *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, which may add map markers for some undiscovered locations. There is also a copy of *[Charwich-Koniinge, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge,_v2 "Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge, v2")* in an open topped crate on the floor and to the left of the shelves are a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). On the lower level, there is a table holding a random potion of stamina and a copy of *[Forge, Hammer and Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge,_Hammer_and_Anvil "Skyrim:Forge, Hammer and Anvil")*. A bench in the opposite corner has a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on top. To the west, in a darkened room is an adept-locked chest. There are stairs leading down to the north.

Halfway along the next corridor, there is an adept-locked door on the left. Behind the door is a makeshift bedroom with a Silver Hand sleeping in the leftmost bed. There are three other beds haphazardly strewn around the room, two end tables and an unlocked chest. On the shelves beside the bed with the bandit there is a random potion of healing and a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide"). On a table in the corner there are three [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"), a [pheasant roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"), three [garlic bulbs](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a random potion of stamina, and a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"). Two garlic braids hang from a cave-in blocked doorway in the north wall.

The corridor leads to the fort's dining and kitchen areas. There are two more Silver Hands here: one across the room by some raised metal spikes, and one to the left sitting at a table, which also holds a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). The table south of this holds an [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a random [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), and a bottle of wine. The table in the southeast of the room has a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top and an unlocked chest beside it. The lever to lower the spikes is directly right of the door, beside the chest. To the south is the kitchen which holds a selection of food items on shelves and in barrels, including three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from racks, with a second pheasant on the floor beneath. Past the metal spikes in the dining room is the door to the cellar.

### Driftshade Cellar

The brewing room

From the entrance, if you head forward, turn left, then left again, you will find some wheat on an end table, and a chest in the dark corner. The other direction leads to a wine cellar. A Silver Hand patrols the next section, past a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall"). A [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") is in the middle of the corridor leading through to the Silver Hand, and on the other side of the trap is a pullbar for manual activation. The reason for this is a bed and chest in a hidden section behind the default position of the spike wall, just pull the handle and the wall will swing open and remain so. You will now have access to the chest.

Past the trap is a small storage area, full of several pieces of iron and leather armor, iron weapons as well as minor potions of stamina and magicka. Down the stairs, there are a random sword and helmet on a table, and a door, which leads to what appear to be a room for brewing mead. There is a Silver Hand either side of the main boiler in the center of the room. Behind the boiler, on the raised section of the room, there is a shelf with minor potions of magicka and health, and a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard")* and another set of shelves holding alto wine and wine against the south wall. There is a tunnel carved into the ice and rock to the north.

There are two more Silver Hands in the first room along the ice tunnel and two apprentice-locked cages, one holding a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") and three [legs of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") and the other holding only a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). You can attack and kill the werewolf in the cage before unlocking the cage, but it will be considered an assault. It will not be considered an assault if you unlock the cage and let the werewolf turn hostile. The next room is guarded by a Silver Hand, and is a torture room. There is more wine on shelves to your left as you enter and a dead werewolf lying in front of a rack. A second table is covered in bloody bones with an iron dagger found among them. After the corridor there is an open doorway into a large room, with stairs down into it on your right. Below you are two Silver Hands by a large fireplace opposite. Behind the fireplace are shelves holding two random skill potions, a coin purse, and an apothecary's satchel with some rarer ingredients. The room has seen better days with fallen masonry and crushed wooden furniture littering various corners of the room. To the south, below where you entered is a candlelit corridor leading to a door back to the refuge.

You enter into a small room with a lit brazier in front of you and a random potion of healing, both on a low table. On your left as you enter, on the south side, are stairs that lead to the final room.

The Silver Hand leader making plans

Behind the barred door is a room with three Silver Hands. They usually gather by the table on the platform to the east with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a piece of [mudcrab chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin"), a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1")*, and (if you are here during the quest [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge")) the [fragments of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragments_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragments of Wuuthrad"). On the table by the fireplace to the south is a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill book *[Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(book) "Skyrim:Warrior (book)")* along with two common books and a coin purse, and behind this a cupboard. The opposite platform is devoid of loose items, but does hold the boss chest, where any items you are sent here to recover may be found. There are also a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") on this platform.

To the south you'll encounter the previously encountered door that was barred at the beginning and you will find yourself at the first room that you've entered through.

## Notes

- Three [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") are near the fort: one north-northeast, one west, and one south-southeast. Two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") are to the east among the rocks south of [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").
- There are a few indicators in the game data that the fort was intended to be named **Driftshade Sanctuary** (the name of the location, the cells' editor IDs, etc.). The exact reason for the change is unknown. The only time the fort is named it is simply called "Driftshade", which offers no insight into the matter.
- Version 2.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces all [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes outside with the snow-covered version of the same plant.
- Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the Silver Hand members here with regular bandits once the dungeon resets, provided that Purity of Revenge is finished.
- Version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") reserves Driftshade Refuge to block radiant quests until after Purity of Revenge is complete. After that point it should switch over to regular bandits and then become available for use in standard radiant questing.

## Bugs

- If the quest [Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)") takes place here at the same time as Purity of Revenge, it may be impossible to complete both quests at once. **?**
- Fast travelling to [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") during Purity of Revenge may automatically complete the optional objective to wipe out the Silver Hand members here, though they may not actually be dead when you arrive.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The bandits at Fort Fellhammer all had a script attached to them when they never needed one.
- The modifications made with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 2.0.9 were incomplete as one of the exterior bandits when the dungeon resets is still a Silver Hand member when it should now be a regular bandit.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. The enemy's base type had to be changed from 'LvlSilverhandMissile\_Aggro1024' to 'LvlBanditMissileAggro1024'.
- After the dungeon respawns, the boss room will sometimes contain two sets of enemies: regular bandits *and* Silver Hand (even if the faction is eradicated). They will be hostile to their counterparts. This can be useful e.g. for obtaining two sets of boss loot at once. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Driftshade Refuge
- 

  Driftshade Cellar

# Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge

## Overview

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Driftshade Refuge

**Driftshade Refuge** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand"). It contains two zones: *[Driftshade Refuge](#Driftshade_Refuge)* and *[Driftshade Cellar](#Driftshade_Cellar)*.

The dilapidated fort, almost lost beneath snowdrifts, is now a base of command for the Silver Hand. Its remote location in the mountains and apparent disappearance from local memory are ideal for concealing activities. It was once a much larger fort, as seen by the broken walls a short distance from the only remaining intact building.

## Related Quests

- **[Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge")**: Retrieve the Fragments of Wuuthrad and wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand").
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are two Silver Hands on guard duty outside the fort. One has lookout duty atop the main building, while the other stands guard by the door. They will warn you against approaching the fort, and turn hostile if you choose to venture too close. To get to the archer on top of the building, you will need to go around the back, where a wooden ramp is located. There are a total of twenty-one snowberry bushes along the path leading up to the front entrance, with two more off to the left of the building, and two more near the cart around the back.

### Driftshade Refuge

The kitchen

After following the stairs down from the entrance, you will come to a multi-junction room. There are two Silver Hands patrolling the middle corridor, which leads to a door that is held shut by a wooden bar on the other side. The eastern corridor has collapsed, so the only option is the western room. Before looting, you may wish to dispose of the Silver Hand in the adjoining room to the right. The first room holds only a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") on the table, and an apothecary's satchel on the top shelf of the second set of shelves from the right. The table to the right in the second room holds a few iron shields and an iron weapon, and a set of shelves to the left holds an assortment of iron weapons. The table to the far left holds a filled random soul gem and a random healing potion.

The next corridor leads to a large two-leveled room. Two more Silver Hands patrol here, one on the top level to the left, and the other straight ahead on the lower level. On the upper level there are several sets of shelves mostly holding [ruined](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and [burned books](/wiki/Skyrim:Burned_Book "Skyrim:Burned Book"), however among these are several common books, a random potion of stamina and *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*, which may add map markers for some undiscovered locations. There is also a copy of *[Charwich-Koniinge, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge,_v2 "Skyrim:Charwich-Koniinge, v2")* in an open topped crate on the floor and to the left of the shelves are a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). On the lower level, there is a table holding a random potion of stamina and a copy of *[Forge, Hammer and Anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge,_Hammer_and_Anvil "Skyrim:Forge, Hammer and Anvil")*. A bench in the opposite corner has a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on top. To the west, in a darkened room is an adept-locked chest. There are stairs leading down to the north.

Halfway along the next corridor, there is an adept-locked door on the left. Behind the door is a makeshift bedroom with a Silver Hand sleeping in the leftmost bed. There are three other beds haphazardly strewn around the room, two end tables and an unlocked chest. On the shelves beside the bed with the bandit there is a random potion of healing and a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide"). On a table in the corner there are three [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot"), a [pheasant roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"), three [garlic bulbs](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a random potion of stamina, and a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"). Two garlic braids hang from a cave-in blocked doorway in the north wall.

The corridor leads to the fort's dining and kitchen areas. There are two more Silver Hands here: one across the room by some raised metal spikes, and one to the left sitting at a table, which also holds a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). The table south of this holds an [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), a random [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), and a bottle of wine. The table in the southeast of the room has a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top and an unlocked chest beside it. The lever to lower the spikes is directly right of the door, beside the chest. To the south is the kitchen which holds a selection of food items on shelves and in barrels, including three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from racks, with a second pheasant on the floor beneath. Past the metal spikes in the dining room is the door to the cellar.

### Driftshade Cellar

The brewing room

From the entrance, if you head forward, turn left, then left again, you will find some wheat on an end table, and a chest in the dark corner. The other direction leads to a wine cellar. A Silver Hand patrols the next section, past a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall"). A [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") is in the middle of the corridor leading through to the Silver Hand, and on the other side of the trap is a pullbar for manual activation. The reason for this is a bed and chest in a hidden section behind the default position of the spike wall, just pull the handle and the wall will swing open and remain so. You will now have access to the chest.

Past the trap is a small storage area, full of several pieces of iron and leather armor, iron weapons as well as minor potions of stamina and magicka. Down the stairs, there are a random sword and helmet on a table, and a door, which leads to what appear to be a room for brewing mead. There is a Silver Hand either side of the main boiler in the center of the room. Behind the boiler, on the raised section of the room, there is a shelf with minor potions of magicka and health, and a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard")* and another set of shelves holding alto wine and wine against the south wall. There is a tunnel carved into the ice and rock to the north.

There are two more Silver Hands in the first room along the ice tunnel and two apprentice-locked cages, one holding a [werewolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") and three [legs of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") and the other holding only a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). You can attack and kill the werewolf in the cage before unlocking the cage, but it will be considered an assault. It will not be considered an assault if you unlock the cage and let the werewolf turn hostile. The next room is guarded by a Silver Hand, and is a torture room. There is more wine on shelves to your left as you enter and a dead werewolf lying in front of a rack. A second table is covered in bloody bones with an iron dagger found among them. After the corridor there is an open doorway into a large room, with stairs down into it on your right. Below you are two Silver Hands by a large fireplace opposite. Behind the fireplace are shelves holding two random skill potions, a coin purse, and an apothecary's satchel with some rarer ingredients. The room has seen better days with fallen masonry and crushed wooden furniture littering various corners of the room. To the south, below where you entered is a candlelit corridor leading to a door back to the refuge.

You enter into a small room with a lit brazier in front of you and a random potion of healing, both on a low table. On your left as you enter, on the south side, are stairs that lead to the final room.

The Silver Hand leader making plans

Behind the barred door is a room with three Silver Hands. They usually gather by the table on the platform to the east with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), a piece of [mudcrab chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin"), a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1")*, and (if you are here during the quest [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge")) the [fragments of Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fragments_of_Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Fragments of Wuuthrad"). On the table by the fireplace to the south is a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill book *[Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(book) "Skyrim:Warrior (book)")* along with two common books and a coin purse, and behind this a cupboard. The opposite platform is devoid of loose items, but does hold the boss chest, where any items you are sent here to recover may be found. There are also a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") on this platform.

To the south you'll encounter the previously encountered door that was barred at the beginning and you will find yourself at the first room that you've entered through.

## Notes

- Three [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") are near the fort: one north-northeast, one west, and one south-southeast. Two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") are to the east among the rocks south of [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").
- There are a few indicators in the game data that the fort was intended to be named **Driftshade Sanctuary** (the name of the location, the cells' editor IDs, etc.). The exact reason for the change is unknown. The only time the fort is named it is simply called "Driftshade", which offers no insight into the matter.
- Version 2.0.8 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces all [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes outside with the snow-covered version of the same plant.
- Version 2.0.9 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") replaces the Silver Hand members here with regular bandits once the dungeon resets, provided that Purity of Revenge is finished.
- Version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") reserves Driftshade Refuge to block radiant quests until after Purity of Revenge is complete. After that point it should switch over to regular bandits and then become available for use in standard radiant questing.

## Bugs

- If the quest [Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)") takes place here at the same time as Purity of Revenge, it may be impossible to complete both quests at once. **?**
- Fast travelling to [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer") during Purity of Revenge may automatically complete the optional objective to wipe out the Silver Hand members here, though they may not actually be dead when you arrive.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The bandits at Fort Fellhammer all had a script attached to them when they never needed one.
- The modifications made with Unofficial Skyrim Patch 2.0.9 were incomplete as one of the exterior bandits when the dungeon resets is still a Silver Hand member when it should now be a regular bandit.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. The enemy's base type had to be changed from 'LvlSilverhandMissile\_Aggro1024' to 'LvlBanditMissileAggro1024'.
- After the dungeon respawns, the boss room will sometimes contain two sets of enemies: regular bandits *and* Silver Hand (even if the faction is eradicated). They will be hostile to their counterparts. This can be useful e.g. for obtaining two sets of boss loot at once. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Driftshade Refuge
- 

  Driftshade Cellar

Dro'marash

**Dro'marash** is a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:TrainerSpeechcraftJourneyman "Skyrim:TrainerSpeechcraftJourneyman") who follows [Ahkari](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahkari "Skyrim:Ahkari")'s [trade caravan](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Khajiit Traders"). He can be found walking the roads between [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), or camped outside either city. He is a common-level [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers") in [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech").

Dro'marash wears a full set of [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), including a pair of steel gauntlets (two variants), and a pair of steel boots (two variants). He is equipped with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") and a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield"), and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

:   **I'd like training in the art of Speech.**
:   *"Well, you've come to the right place."*

# Skyrim:Drovas Relvi

## Overview

| Drovas Relvi (RefID: [xx](/wiki/Skyrim:Form_ID "Skyrim:Form ID")01843D) | | | |

Drovas Relvi

**Drovas Relvi** is a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") who works as a cook at [the Retching Netch](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Retching_Netch "Skyrim:The Retching Netch") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). He works for [Geldis Sadri](/wiki/Skyrim:Geldis_Sadri "Skyrim:Geldis Sadri"). He relocates to [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)") after completing the quest [Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward").

When he moves to Tel Mithryn, he will live at Tel Mithryn Steward's House, and he'll have the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_Key "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's Key") to the house added to his inventory, along with starting an entirely new daily routine. He will start his day in his house at 6am, and stay there for two hours. Then at 8am, he'll head over to the [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Apothecary "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Apothecary") to visit [Elynea](/wiki/Skyrim:Elynea_Mothren "Skyrim:Elynea Mothren") for an hour. He will then head to the [kitchen](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Kitchen "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Kitchen") to visit [Ulves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulves_Romoran "Skyrim:Ulves Romoran") for an hour. He will then head up to the main [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") to check on Neloth for an hour. He will go outside the tower to get some air for an hour. After that, at noon, he'll head back to his house to eat a one-hour lunch. When he's finished, at 1pm, he'll go outside for an hour. Then at 2pm, he'll visit Elynea again for an hour. After that, at 3pm, he'll once again visit Ulves for an hour. Then he'll go outside, once again, for an hour. He'll then, at 5pm, once again check on Neloth for an hour. Then at 6pm, he'll go home and eat dinner for an hour. At 7pm, when he's done with dinner, he'll give Elynea one last hour-long visit, then head home. Then at 10pm he'll head to work on the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") for eight hours, or, if the stone has been [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), he'll sleep in his house indefinitely (see [bugs](#Bugs)). The only exception to his routine is if you still haven't completed [From the Ashes](/wiki/Skyrim:From_the_Ashes "Skyrim:From the Ashes"); then he will stay in his house until the quest is completed.

Drovas wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0006c1da "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000261bd "Skyrim:Boots"). He carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and a small amount of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Reluctant Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Reluctant_Steward "Skyrim:Reluctant Steward")**: Find a new steward for [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[A New Debt](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Debt "Skyrim:A New Debt")**: Help Drovas Relvi with his debt to [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)").
- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").

### Raven Rock

His greetings:

:   *"Welcome to the Retching Netch Cornerclub, milord/milady. If you need anything, Master Geldis will be happy to help you"*
:   *"We have all sorts of authentic dark elf food and drink here. Geldis spares no expense"*
:   *"Geldis may be a tough boss, but I can put up with it. Keeps a roof over my head."*
:   *"I don't mind working at the Retching Netch, but I was hoping for a bit more when I moved to Solstheim. Ah well"*
:   *"There's got to be more to life than sweeping and cleaning all day."*

### Raven Rock Conversations

In the Retching Netch, he can be seen conversing with his boss, Geldis:

**Geldis**: *"Drovas, I thought I told you I needed the jazbay crushed for my Emberbrand Wine. Where is it?"*
**Drovas**: *"We ran out of jazbay berries almost two weeks ago."*
**Geldis**: *"Damn it. I wish you would have told me sooner."*
**Drovas**: *"Sorry, boss."*

**Geldis**: *"Drovas! I need you to clean the rooms again. I went through there, and there's ash everywhere."*
**Drovas**: *"Sorry, boss. The ash comes in faster than I can clean it up."*
**Geldis**: *"Well, then you'll just have to clean them twice a day. Whatever it takes."*
**Drovas**: *"Yes, boss."*

### Tel Mithryn

His greetings:

:   *"After what you did for me, you are always welcome here. Just try to stay out of Master Neloth's way"*
:   *"I can't thank you enough for setting me up as steward of Tel Mithryn"*
:   *"Neloth may be crazy, but it's better than staying in Raven Rock."*
:   *"Master Neloth certainly keeps me busy. Taking care of this estate is a lot of work."*
:   *"I just can't seem to get the hang of making a decent cup of canis root tea."*
:   *"I hope Elynea has something to help me sleep at night."*
:   *"I heard you fought a dragon. That must have been terrifying."* **(Completed [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising"))**
:   *"Working on those standing stones feels like a bad dream. I'm glad you woke us from it."*

If spoken to:

:   **How are you getting along here?**
:   *"Neloth is a real task master. And the tea. The thrice damned tea! I don't think I'll ever learn to make it properly."*

When released from the Sun Stone:

:   *"Who did this to us? It isn't another one of Master Neloth's games, is it?"*
:   *"I... I must have been drugged. That's it. Someone drugged me. Maybe one of Mogrul's cronies."*

### Tel Mithryn Conversations

He can now also be seen having the following conversations with other Tel Mithryn residents:

**Drovas**: *"Master Neloth, the silt strider traders just dropped off some supplies."*
**Neloth**: *"What did they bring? Books? Soul gems?"*
**Drovas**: *"Mostly books. There were a couple of soul gems, some ingredients for Elynea, and some strange wood."*
**Neloth**: *"Ah! The wood is for the staffs. Put them away when you get a chance. But don't get in my way."*

**Neloth**: *"Drovas, where's my tea?"*
**Drovas**: *"I'll go fetch some, Master Neloth. Canis root, right?"*
**Neloth**: *"Yes, yes. Canis root tea. And don't let Ulves water it down."*

**Drovas**: *"How are your ears, Talvas?"*
**Talvas**: *"They're back to regular size. It didn't hurt nearly as much this time."*
**Drovas**: *"I don't understand why you let him do these things to you."*
**Talvas**: *"Master Neloth is the most powerful wizard of House Telvanni. Maybe the most powerful in all of Morrowind. Someday I will inherit all of this. It's worth a little pain."*

**Talvas**: *"Master Neloth is preparing to... well, it's better if you don't know. However, if you hear unearthly screams, I would advise you to not come up."*
**Drovas**: *"Unearthly screams? What have I gotten myself into."*
**Talvas**: *"You better get used to this, Drovas. This isn't that unusual for Tel Mithryn."*
**Drovas**: *"I know, I know. So, unearthly screams, don't come up. Got it."*

**Drovas**: *"Do you ever get lonely out here in the middle of nowhere?"*
**Elynea**: *"You complain too much. Tel Mithryn is the safest place in Solstheim. Only a fool would challenge Master Neloth."*
**Drovas**: *"I suppose you're right. At least here I'm safe from Mogrul."*

**Elynea**: *"I miss Varona. She used to help me with the gardening."*
**Drovas**: *"I can't help it if I have a black thumb. It's like the mushrooms hate me."*
**Elynea**: *"It's not your fault, Drovas. You do other things well. Varona was never able to do the repair work that you do."*
**Drovas**: *"Thank you. I didn't mean to be so defensive. I know Varona was your friend. It's okay to miss her."*

### Dragonborn

During [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)"):

:   **What's being built outside of town?**
:   *"Do you mean by the Earth Stone? There's a shrine there, but I don't remember what it's for..."*
:   **Can you tell me more about the shrine outside of town?**
:   *"Well, I... You know, I can't remember. It's important, I think, but it's hard for me to think about."*

When asked if he knows someone named [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)"):

:   **Do you know someone called Miraak?**
:   *"Did I know someone by that name? Someone... Someone that wanted something..."*
:   **What does that mean?**
:   *"Maybe I'm just confused. I can't be sure."*

### It's All In The Taste

During [It's All In The Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:It%27s_All_In_The_Taste "Skyrim:It's All In The Taste"), if you offer him some of [Geldis' sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sadri%27s_Sujamma "Skyrim:Sadri's Sujamma"), he'll decline:

:   **Geldis Sadri wants you to try his new drink.**
:   *"Sorry, Geldis won't allow me to drink while I'm working at the Netch."*

### Reluctant Steward

When [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") finds out his [old steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas") is dead, he sends you to Raven Rock to find a new steward. When asked if he wants the job

:   **Do you want to become the new steward of Tel Mithryn?**
:   *"Uh... you mean leave Raven Rock? For good? To go work for a crazed Telvanni wizard? Sure. Just let me get my things. On second thought, nevermind. I can get new stuff."*
:   **You seem awfully eager.**
:   *"Well, I've never been one to pass up an opportunity. Sorry to run, but I'm off to my new job."*

He will then leave the Retching Netch and Raven Rock for good, running all the way to Tel Mithryn to start his new job. If you try to converse with him when he's making the trip to Tel Mithryn, he will only say:

:   *"I'm off to take up my new position with Master Neloth."*

### A New Debt

After setting Drovas up as steward, when you head back to Raven Rock, [Mogrul](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogrul_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Mogrul (Dragonborn)") will approach you saying Drovas owed him one-thousand septims, and that since you were the one to make him untouchable, the debt is now yours. You can now ask Drovas if he owed Mogrul money:

:   **Do you owe Mogrul money?**
:   *"Uh...Well, sort of. I owed him a thousand septims, but not any more. He doesn't dare try to collect now that I'm Neloth's steward."*
:   **Except now he expects me to pay him.**
:   *"Wow. Sorry about that. He's never going to stop you know. He'll keep sending thugs after you until either you pay him or kill him."*
:   **Why don't you just pay him?**
:   *"Pay him? Why? I mean, I don't have the money. Well, I might soon. Neloth does pay well. But the important thing is that I don't have it. In fact, it's not likely I'll ever have it. Expenses you know. Sorry about the thugs and Mogrul and everything."*

If you exit the conversation now and once again ask him if he owes Mogrul money, he'll say:

:   *"I already told you, Mogrul can't touch me now. Whatever is between you and Mogrul is your problem."*

You'll now only have one option to persuade. Note that you need a [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill of 75 to successfully persuade him:

| Option | Dialogue | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **You should pay me what you can. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Well... I... Oh, fine. Here. This is all I have."* **Failed**: *"I don't see why. He's your problem now."* | **Passed**: Get 250 gold **Failed**: Nothing |

During the quest, when exiting conversation he can say:

:   *"Mogrul isn't someone you can ignore."*

After the quest, if you paid off his debt:

:   *"I heard you paid my debt to Mogrul. I don't know how I can every*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *repay you."*

If you killed Mogrul:

:   *"I heard Mogrul is dead. That is a relief!"*

## Bugs

- If he has become a steward and the [Sun Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Stone "Skyrim:Sun Stone") has been cleansed, his sleep package will always be active, and therefore he will be found sleeping indefinitely in [Tel Mithryn Steward's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_Steward%27s_House "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn Steward's House").
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.
- If he becomes a steward and the Sun Stone has been cleansed, his sleep package may still have him trying to sleep at the Retching Netch, even though he doesn't work there anymore.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Drowned Sorrows

## Overview

[Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") drowning his sorrows

## Quick Walkthrough

**Note**: This quest does not appear in your journal.

1. Speak with [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran") and deal with [Ranmir's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") debt.
2. Speak with Dagur about Ranmir.
3. Speak to Ranmir and then Haran again to learn that [Isabelle](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine") went to see [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
4. Talk to Vex in the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon").
5. Find Isabelle Rolaine in [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave").
6. Return to Ranmir with [her note](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Isabelle's Letter").

### The Great Collapse

Ever since the [Great Collapse](/wiki/Lore:Great_Collapse "Lore:Great Collapse"), the once prosperous town of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") has been in a state of disarray, with only a few inhabitants left. The only remaining merchant, [Birna](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna"), and her brother [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") have both felt the agony in the wake of the Collapse, as most of the townsfolk are long gone, providing little income for the family store. When you visit Winterhold for the first time, you will witness an [argument](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Barrow#Birna.27s_Odd_Investment "Skyrim:Yngol's Barrow") between the two in the middle of the street, and they will continue inside local inn [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth"):

*"Please, come home. Just... Just come home."*

**Birna**: *"Please, come home. Just... Just come home."*
**Ranmir**: *"Can't. Got at least two rounds to go. Why don't you go... sell something."*
**Birna**: *"Why? Because I'd rather be here trying to keep my only brother from drinking himself to death."*
**Ranmir**: *"Ha! Drink ain't gonna kill me. Not today, anyway."*

While Birna keeps her store open for nobody, Ranmir proceeds to down mead around the clock inside the Frozen Hearth, seemingly falling apart, much to the dismay of the innkeeper, [Dagur](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagur "Skyrim:Dagur") and waitress [Haran](/wiki/Skyrim:Haran "Skyrim:Haran"). When listening in on their conversations, however, it becomes apparent that there may be another reason Ranmir became the town drunk:

**Haran**: *"How long are we going to let Ranmir drink himself into a stupor? When will enough be enough?"*
**Dagur**: *"As long as he keeps paying, I suppose. He keeps to himself, and isn't hurting anyone."*
**Haran**: *"Are you so sure of that? I think Birna might disagree with you."*
**Dagur**: *"It's not my place to get involved in their family's business, remember? You're the one that told me to stay out of it."*

### The Concerned Innkeeper

*"How long are we going to let Ranmir drink himself into a stupor?"*

After helping Ranmir [pay his debts](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Few_Words_with_You#Haran_and_Ranmir "Skyrim:A Few Words with You") to Haran, concerned innkeeper Dagur will have a new dialogue option, namely asking if there is anything to do around the inn. Dagur will then tell you about the very reason Ranmir became the town drunk: *"Listen, we're friends, right? I wondered if I could ask a favor of you. It's about Ranmir. Don't get me wrong, I don't have a problem with him being here all the time. He mostly keeps to himself, and so far he's been able to pay. I just hate to see what's happened to him. He hasn't always been like this, you know. Drunk, I mean."* He then proceeds to tell you about Ranmir's broken heart: *"Oh, he was a different person. Happy, outgoing... Like anyone who's in love. See, Ranmir was involved with a pretty young woman named Isabelle Rolaine. The two of them were very happy together, I thought. One day, she just disappeared. Ranmir was convinced she'd run off with someone else, leaving him behind. He turned to drinking, and what's left of him is what you see here every day."* He then reasons that if Isabelle could be found, Ranmir could get some peace of mind and get his act back together. When asked about Isabelle, Ranmir will get overly insulted, saying: *"Don't you... Don't you say that name to me. Don't you dare. Ever."* Luckily, the equally concerned Haran has a bit of information on Isabelle's whereabouts, although she will hint that Isabelle is hanging out with a bad crowd: *"It's none of your business. Those aren't folks you want to get tangled up with."* She will then explain the danger: *"One night Ranmir was in here like always, drinking himself to death. When I told him there was no more Honningbrew, that he'd drank it all, he got angry. He ranted at me, how I didn't know what he's been through, how Isabelle broke his heart when she ran off with some thief named Vex..."*

### Vex

If you are a member of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), you already know master infiltrator [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex"). She can always be found hanging out at the [Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon"). If you have completed [Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business"), she will even talk to you, and you will have the option to ask her about Isabelle Rolaine. When confronted with the name Ranmir, she will get exasperated: *"Not him again. He came nosing around Riften a while back, making a lot of noise about me. He was... persuaded to leave before he found me. Funny, I'd have thought she would've gone back to him by now."* Once she reveals she knew Isabelle, she will say: *"She came through a while ago, wanted to know where she could get her hands on something valuable. Anything, really. I told her it was a bad idea, that she wasn't cut out for what'd be necessary, but she wouldn't hear it. So I gave her some advice, pointed her towards Hobs*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *Fall Cave and that was that."*

### Drowned Sorrows

[Isabelle Rolaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle_Rolaine "Skyrim:Isabelle Rolaine")

[Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave") is a small cave between [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and Ranmir's hometown, Winterhold. According to Vex, Isabelle went there to seek out treasure from the residing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), but never made it far. As you approach the cave, stains of blood will lead to the entrance and right inside, you will find Isabelle leaning against a rock, dead. Examine her body and you will find [her letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Isabelle%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Isabelle's Letter"), her own full explanation for leaving her beloved Ranmir behind and seeking a fortune in a remote cave: *"I know it's been hard on you, on both of us, struggling to survive. I hate to see the look in your eyes every time you think about how little the two of us have, and I know you're too proud to ever say anything. So I'm going to make it all better."* Return to Ranmir and hand him the letter and watch while he reads it: *"Don't you go pulling my leg. Give it here. This... This is really from her, isn't it? Did she really run off and do this? For me? By the Eight. She's dead, isn't she? And it's all my fault. I... I have some thinking to do. Thank you for this."* Ranmir will then leave the Frozen Hearth, and vanish.

## Notes

- The note is not marked as a quest item, and can be dropped like any normal item. This quest can become impossible to complete if you lose track of the note.
- If you enter Hob's Fall Cave before getting this quest, Isabelle's body is not there yet.
- It is not necessary to speak to Ranmir or Vex. Once the quest is started the body appears in the cave.
- There are several radiant quests that may use this cave. They can all be done simultaneously.
- Ranmir disappears from the game after the quest (once you visit Winterhold exterior).
- The Unofficial Patch adds objectives to this quest.

## Bugs

- If Ranmir dies while this quest is running, it will appear to proceed normally except that you'll never be able to complete it. The last objective will be displayed with no map marker.
  -  Use the following series of console commands to resurrect Ranmir and finish the quest:

:   :   :   ```
            prid 1c18b
            moveto player
            resurrect
            ```

- The quest marker on your map may not show up, nor will it appear anywhere in your journal. Despite this, the quest itself will still be very much active once you talk to Haran.
- Sometimes Isabelle's body can be found in Hob's Fall Cave before getting the quest, but she doesn't have a note yet. **?**
- Isabelle may be found in the cave without any clothes.
- [Birna's](/wiki/Skyrim:Birna "Skyrim:Birna") dialogue after the end of Drowned Sorrows doesn't change to mention that [Ranmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranmir "Skyrim:Ranmir") is gone.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- Isabelle's Letter isn't marked as a quest item for Drowned Sorrows, which can cause the quest to become permanently stuck if the letter is lost before the quest is finished.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, addresses this issue. The letter is now marked as a quest item until the quest is finished.

## Quest Stages

- All of the quest stages are empty: 0, 10, 20, 30, 40.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformWinterholdC stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformWinterholdC`.

# Skyrim:Druadach Mountains

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Landmark: Druadach Mountains ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Druadach+Mountains)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Druadach_Mountains "Lore:Druadach Mountains")) | | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Westernmost Skyrim | |

The Druadach Mountains

The **Druadach Mountains** are a mountain range in western [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") serving as a natural barrier to separate [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") from [High Rock](/wiki/Lore:High_Rock "Lore:High Rock") and [Hammerfell](/wiki/Lore:Hammerfell "Lore:Hammerfell").

The range curves from the northeast around [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") to [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"). The misty peaks tower over [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") and [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") in [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), though they gradually diminish closer to [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") and [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). The [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") originates in the range and drops down many waterfalls as it flows to the northeast following the range to the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). Since the [First Era](/wiki/Lore:First_Era "Lore:First Era"), the [Reachmen](/wiki/Lore:Reachmen "Lore:Reachmen"), now known as the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), have been taking advantage of the cliffs, caves, and rugged terrain of the Druadach Mountains in guerrilla warfare campaigns against invading armies. The range is home to many ancient [Dwemer ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwemer Ruins"), [Nord fortresses](/wiki/Skyrim:Forts "Skyrim:Forts"), and [Orc strongholds](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds").

# Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
