Druadach Redoubt

**Druadach Redoubt** is a small [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") and cave south of [Mor Khazgur](/wiki/Skyrim:Mor_Khazgur "Skyrim:Mor Khazgur"). It contains only one zone, *[Druadach Redoubt Cave](#Druadach_Redoubt_Cave)*.

If you sided with the Forsworn in the quest [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine"), [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach") can be found here and the Forsworn occupying the camp will not attack you, although the Forsworn in the exterior zone may still come to blows with your horse, dog, or other pet.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Borkul the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Borkul_the_Beast "Skyrim:Borkul the Beast")\*  [Braig](/wiki/Skyrim:Braig "Skyrim:Braig")\*  [Duach](/wiki/Skyrim:Duach "Skyrim:Duach")\*  [Kaie](/wiki/Skyrim:Kaie "Skyrim:Kaie")\*  [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach")\*  [Odvan](/wiki/Skyrim:Odvan "Skyrim:Odvan")\*  [Uraccen](/wiki/Skyrim:Uraccen "Skyrim:Uraccen")\* |

\* Present if they survive the quest [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine"). In addition to these NPCs, there are two leveled melee Forsworn (one will be at the farm and the other in the middle tier), two leveled archer Forsworn (one will be in the middle tier and the other on the highest tier), and one [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") (on the highest tier).

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Along the path leading to the camp is a tall tree with a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") on the ground under it and a set of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from it. The exterior of the redoubt is home to a small camp of Forsworn. There are only two leveled Forsworn (one melee and one archer) in the camp outside for you to deal with before moving into the interior of the redoubt. The camp includes a single tent containing a [pile of hay](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping "Skyrim:Sleeping") that can be used for sleeping and a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plant. To the left of the tent is a tree stump with [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on it. There is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") upstream from the camp on the southern shore near a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant, and three growths of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") fungus and another nightshade are on either side of the entrance to the cave, with more nightshade, [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"), and [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") growing around the camp.

### Druadach Redoubt Cave

Cave interior

Upon entering there is a short tunnel with an iron ore vein on your left before emerging into the main cave; you will then have to cross a small stream via a bridge. The cave consists of three ascending ledges, with two paths leading up to the rear of the cave. On your left as your cross the bridge is a row of weapon racks holding a [Forsworn bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Bow "Skyrim:Forsworn Bow") and [axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Axe "Skyrim:Forsworn Axe"). Alternatively you can try and sneak around the bridge and onto the other side. After you have crossed the bridge there is a small farm consisting of fourteen potato plants, a [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), a [grain mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Milling "Skyrim:Milling"), and a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood"), which is tended to by a single Forsworn. There is a table near the mill with a basket containing potatoes and a [Forsworn sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Sword "Skyrim:Forsworn Sword") on top. To the right of the wood chopping block is a rack holding three [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). To the left of these are several barrels and sacks mostly containing food; however, one of the barrels holds ingredients. There are two [quicksilver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") along the northern wall beside the potato plants.

Reach map

If you follow the ramp up from the farm you will encounter the largest tier of the redoubt. Immediately on your left, on a ledge, there is a [shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay") surrounded by candles. Despite being the largest tier, there are only two Forsworn for you to dispatch; one of these may be sleeping in the tent on the left, above the farm, while the other patrols the other end of the level. To the right of the tent is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") under an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") and bone chimes hanging from a tree. There is a level-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") just to the right of the easternmost wooden ramp that leads up to the top tier. It is partially hidden by plant matter and is set back under the top tier, below a [Juniper tree](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper "Skyrim:Juniper"). On either side of the other path up to the middle tier are large tents, both of which have hay piles inside; one contains a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide") and a random [healing potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), while the other contains a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide"). Against the southwest wall, just before the southern ramp up to the highest tier, is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack").

Climbing the southern ramp from the middle tier, you will have reached the highest tier of the redoubt, where the boss Forsworn lurks often working at a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") near the northern ramp up to the top level. There are three [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot") resting on the forge. (If you have completed [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine"), it will be as easy as sneak-killing them, as all the NPCs in the redoubt will be friendly if you sided with Madanach.) On your right is another large tent containing a hay pile, with a sleeping leveled Forsworn. Beyond this there is a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") to the right of a cage among the plant matter. In the center of this level is a campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") hanging over it. Next to the fire is a long wooden table holding a selection of meats.

Against the rear wall of the cave is a second tanning rack. To the left of this is another tent containing an unlocked chest (where any items you are sent here to recover will be found). Toward the front of this tier, against a large pillar of rock and west of the campfire, is a set of shelves holding a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Rear Guard](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rear_Guard "Skyrim:The Rear Guard")*, a random [magicka potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a deer hide, and some more raw meats. To the right of the shelves on the ground is a [wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt"). Against the northeast wall of the cave is a long wooden table with a map of the Reach showing the locations of all Forsworn camps, a random enchanted [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") (see [bugs](#Bugs)), four loose [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins, two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick"), and a deer hide on top. Activating the map plots the locations of any undiscovered Forsworn camps on your world map, after which the map disappears from the table.

## Notes

- The grain mill can be used to produce [flour](/wiki/Skyrim:Sack_of_Flour "Skyrim:Sack of Flour")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") from [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") if [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") is installed.
- Because the inhabitants are friendly after completing No One Escapes Cidhna Mine if you side with Madanach, any radiant quests that send you here can be easily completed by killing the target and walking back out through the front entrance. Oddly, the friendly inhabitants do not attack you even if you kill the Briarheart in plain view.
  - If you want to avoid combat completely, you can also pickpocket the [briar heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart") from the target, which will instantly kill him. This is considerably easier than performing the same actions in other locations as the target in question is not hostile to you, eliminating any need to sneak up to him to avoid combat before picking his pocket.
  - The guards at the redoubt will all remain friendly even if neither Madanach nor any of his group actually escape Markarth alive, so long as you choose to side with them initially during the quest No One Escapes Cidhna Mine.

## Bugs

- Druadach Redoubt isn't marked as a cave, so cave-based radiant quests won't target it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- One of the food sacks beneath the skill book can not be interacted with.
- The enchanted dagger may clip through the table and be located beneath the ground under the table; however, careful searching should enable it to be found. **?**
- While the generic Forsworn may be non-hostile to you after siding with [Madanach](/wiki/Skyrim:Madanach "Skyrim:Madanach") during [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine"), they will still attack animals or other special followers you have with you on sight. This applies to all dogs (including [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas")), the [Dremora Butler](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Butler "Skyrim:Dremora Butler"), and any pets added by Creations, such as the [Dwarven Armored Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)") and [Nix-Hound](/wiki/Skyrim:Nix-Hound_(creature) "Skyrim:Nix-Hound (creature)"). This is due to these followers not being added to the "[DruadachRedoubtFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction "Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction")", unlike the player and other humanoid followers.
  -  Adding them to the [DruadachRedoubtFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction "Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction") faction (RefID `E3609`) will fix this problem.
- The anvil next to the forge is actually a separate anvil (like those found at Imperial and Stormcloak [military camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Camps "Skyrim:Military Camps")), not an anvil that is part of a regular forge (like that seen outside [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")). If you interact with the anvil, you can smith things normally, but if you interact with the forge basin, the smithing menu will briefly open before you are "transferred" to the anvil and the menu opens again. This placement of two forging objects close together is presumably an error. **?**
- Mining ore from the quicksilver ore vein directly across from the grain mill (by activating it, not attacking it with a pickaxe) results in a camera placement where you are stuck looking at the stone wall (with your character not visible at all) until the mining animation is finished. The other quicksilver ore vein does not exhibit this bug. **?**
- The goat here will often be killed by one of the Forsworn members.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.3, addresses this issue. This was due to improperly set faction relationships between "DruadachRedoubtFaction" and "GoatFaction". The relationships between them have been set to friend.

## Maps

- 

  Druadach Redoubt Cave

Dryston

**Dryston** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [barbarian](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbarian "Skyrim:Barbarian") working for the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). During the related quest he tries to beat you up after you nose around too much.

After receiving his beating, Dryston will take up residence in [Weylin](/wiki/Skyrim:Weylin "Skyrim:Weylin")'s old room in [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"), where he will remain for the rest of the game, offering no unique dialogue. The room itself will still be identified as Weylin's room, and Weylin's room key will unlock the door as normal.

Dryston wears a set of [leather armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Leather Armor") with a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"). He is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a selection of [lower-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").

## Quest-Related Events

After you exit the Warrens he will confront you and say:

:   *"You've been digging around where you don't belong. It's time you learned a lesson."*

If you've lost the brawl to him once before he will instead say:

:   *"You again. Guess you need another lesson, huh?"*

| Topic | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| **You first. (Brawl)** | *"Let's go!"* |
| **Who sent you?** | *"Someone who doesn't like you asking questions."* |
| **I don't listen to threats.** | *"You'll listen to this."* |

After you beat him in a brawl on the streets he will fall to the ground while gasping for air and mutter:

:   *"Ugh. You mangy piece of pit-bait!"*
:   **Talk, or I send you to the gods.**
:   *"I was sent by [Nepos the Nose](/wiki/Skyrim:Nepos_the_Nose "Skyrim:Nepos the Nose"). The old man hands out the orders. He told me to make sure you didn't get in the way. That's all I know, I swear!"*

Any further attempts to speak with him will just result in him saying:

:   *"Nepos is in charge. That's all I know."*

## Notes

- If he dies before telling you about Nepos the Nose, you can find [a note](/wiki/Skyrim:Dryston%27s_Note "Skyrim:Dryston's Note") on his corpse addressed to a friend. It explains that Nepos ordered him to rough you up. His note refers to you as "him" regardless of your actual gender.

# Skyrim:Duach

## Overview

| Duach (RefID: 00019912) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | | |
| Location | [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), then [Druadach Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Redoubt "Skyrim:Druadach Redoubt") | | |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |
| Level | PC×0.5 (max=30) | Class | [Witchblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchblade "Skyrim:Witchblade") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019912 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00013393 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 25+(PC-2)×5 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50+(PC-2)×2.5 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") | | |
| Perks | [MS02IncreaseDamage](/wiki/Skyrim:MS02IncreaseDamage "Skyrim:MS02IncreaseDamage"); [Reduce Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Reduce_Damage "Skyrim:Reduce Damage") | | |

| Voice Type | [MaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommoner") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionCidhnaMine](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionCidhnaMine "Skyrim:CrimeFactionCidhnaMine"); [DruadachRedoubtFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction "Skyrim:DruadachRedoubtFaction"); [TownCidhnaMinePrisonerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownCidhnaMinePrisonerFaction "Skyrim:TownCidhnaMinePrisonerFaction") | | |

Duach

**Duach** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [witchblade](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchblade "Skyrim:Witchblade") held prisoner in [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"). It is unknown exactly how long he has been there, but it is believed that it has been around seven years since he has seen daylight. He will make no secret of his hatred for the Nords.

He also has a bottle of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") with him that [Grisvar the Unlucky](/wiki/Skyrim:Grisvar_the_Unlucky "Skyrim:Grisvar the Unlucky") asks you to take in exchange for a [shiv](/wiki/Skyrim:Shiv "Skyrim:Shiv").

## Related Quests

- **[No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine")**: Escape from [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine")!

### No One Escapes Cidhna Mine

When approached he can say:

:   *"Whenever I get out of here, I'm going to go kill a Nord."*
:   *"Other prisoners get suspicious when we talk to each other, so keep it down."*

You will need to get skooma off of him to get the shiv from Grisvar:

:   **I hear you have some skooma.**
:   *"You give me one more look, and I cut you open. That Skooma's mine."*

:   :   **Never mind.**

        :   *"Smart."*

:   :   **I need some. Badly. (Persuade)**

        :   *"Getting the shakes, huh? All right. Take it. Old gods keep you."* (Success)
        :   *"Skooma addict. Get lost."* (Failure)

:   :   **Hand over the skooma. (Intimidate)**

        :   *"Easy there. I didn't mean nothing. Take it."* (Success)
        :   *"That's it."* (Failure that will lead to a brawl)

After this little fight if you failed to intimidate him, he will be rather annoyed and mumble:

:   *"Damn addicts always stealing from me. Here. I hope you choke on it."*

He can be asked questions about himself:

:   **How long have you been here?**
:   *"Year seven, I think? Surprised I haven't cut my own throat out by now, but something keeps me going."*
:   **What are you in for?**
:   *"I'm a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). One of our raids went bad, and I got captured. Would've been fine dying for the [Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") with my kinsmen, but the Silver-Bloods want their ore mined, so they threw me in here."*

While escaping the mine, if you speak to him he will say:

:   *"Come on, move it. We have Nords to kill."*

## Conversations

Throughout the day, Duach can be seen talking to his fellow prisoners:

:   **Braigh**: *"Think the guards will be coming down, soon?"*
:   **Duach**: *"Ah, it's not been more than a few days since they came down the last time."*

:   **Braigh**: *"Nearly broke my back out in the mines today. Damn Nords should bleed for putting us through this!"*
:   **Duach**: *"Some day, brother. Some day."*

:   **Odvan**: *"Think maybe we should jump the guards when they come down next?"*
:   **Duach**: *"They keep the doors locked when they come down. You kill them, you're trapping us here with no food."*

This scene, despite mentioning Odvan's alias in Braig's stead, is actually set up to work with Braig and Duach.

:   **Braig**: *"Have any skooma? I need to get something from Grisvar."*
:   **Duach**: *"You make one move towards my skooma, and I shiv you."*

## Spells

Duach knows the following spells:

- [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration")
  - [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh")
- [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration")
  - [Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie")
- [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")
  - [Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Flames "Skyrim:Flames")

## Notes

- Duach, despite being a member of the Forsworn before he came into Cidhna Mine, does not possess their trademark face tattoos. He shares this quirk with [Kaie](/wiki/Skyrim:Kaie "Skyrim:Kaie") and some of his fellow prisoners.

# Skyrim:Dulug

## Overview

| Dulug (RefID: 000C78C1) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Stronghold | [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal") | | |

| Other Information | | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Blood-Kin of the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood-Kin_of_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Blood-Kin of the Orcs"); [GuardFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardFaction_(makes_an_actor_a_guard) "Skyrim:GuardFaction (makes an actor a guard)"); [TownDushnikhYalFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownDushnikhYalFaction "Skyrim:TownDushnikhYalFaction"); [Tribal Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribal_Orcs "Skyrim:Tribal Orcs") | | |

Dulug taking a break in the mine

**Dulug** is an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:GuardOrc1H "Skyrim:GuardOrc1H") living in [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"), the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). She works in [Dushnikh Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Mine "Skyrim:Dushnikh Mine"), mining [orichalcum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore") along with [Ghak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghak "Skyrim:Ghak"), [Mahk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mahk "Skyrim:Mahk"), and [Oglub](/wiki/Skyrim:Oglub "Skyrim:Oglub").

Dulug spends her entire life inside the mine and never sleeps. She divides her time between hacking away on the ore veins, relaxing, or eating.

She wears simple clothing, a pair of [ragged trousers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Trousers "Skyrim:Ragged Trousers") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#00080699 "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries her [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a leveled [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Key to Burguk's Longhouse") to [Burguk's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Burguk's Longhouse"), along with a selection of [middle-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

:   *"I'm here to mine, outlander. So unless you want to dig, get out."*
:   *"I have metal to dig."*
:   *"Malacath has given me the task to mine. Good ore brings strength to our people."*
:   *"Every Orc learns the heavy labor of mining. All spend years in the caves."*
:   *"The mines are hard, but Malacath rewards those who rise to the challenge."*

# Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Bandits)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | Two skill boosts |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 (Quest Giver) |
| ID: | Favor204 |

.jpg)

Amren and his wife arguing

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from either of the following people. The dungeon is randomly determined from the Bandit Camps present in the quest giver's hold.

| Region | Location | Quest Giver | Quest Item | Dialogue Trigger | Reward | Dungeon(s) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Argonian Assemblage](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Assemblage "Skyrim:Argonian Assemblage") | [Shahvee](/wiki/Skyrim:Shahvee "Skyrim:Shahvee") | [Shahvee's Amulet of Zenithar](#Shahvee.27s_Amulet_of_Zenithar) | "Your people have bad luck?" | +1 to [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") and [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") | [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern"), [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock"), [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"), [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Amren's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren%27s_House "Skyrim:Amren's House") | [Amren](/wiki/Skyrim:Amren "Skyrim:Amren") | [Amren's Family Sword](#Amren.27s_Family_Sword) | "What were you two arguing about?" | +1 to [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") and [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") | [Halted Stream Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Halted_Stream_Camp "Skyrim:Halted Stream Camp"), [Redoran's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Redoran's Retreat"), [Swindler's Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Swindler%27s_Den "Skyrim:Swindler's Den"), [Valtheim Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Keep "Skyrim:Valtheim Keep"), [White River Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River_Watch "Skyrim:White River Watch") |

## Detailed Walkthrough

It is a standard fetch-and-return quest. The item will be found in the boss chest in the target dungeon, and is treated as a [quest item](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items "Skyrim:Quest Items").

### Amren's Family Sword

When you encounter Amren, he may be arguing with his wife [Saffir](/wiki/Skyrim:Saffir "Skyrim:Saffir"). If asked about the argument, Amren will tell you about his father's sword:

:   *My Saffir doesn't like that I've been spending so much time looking for my father's old sword. He fed his entire family with the gold he made using that weapon. I'm not about to let it gather dust in some thief's trophy room.*

Volunteering to retrieve the sword for him triggers the start of the quest.

| Name | ID | Type | [Damage](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Heavy_Attack.png "Damage") | [Weight](/wiki/File:SR-icon-clothing-Leather_Backpack_(square).png "Weight") | [Value](/wiki/File:SR-item-Gold-heads.png "Value") |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Amren's Family Sword | 000647ac | 1 Hand Sword | 7 | 9 | 25 |

When you return the sword, Amren gives you a one point bonus in both [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") and [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed"), commenting, "*Here, my father had a favorite sword and shield technique. Let me teach it to you, in honor of his memory.*"

### Shahvee's Amulet of Zenithar

If you talk to Shahvee you may have the option to ask her, "Your people have bad luck?" In response she will tell you:

:   *We have not faired*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *well outside our native [Black Marsh](/wiki/Lore:Black_Marsh "Lore:Black Marsh"), but we're determined to make the best of things. I began praying to [Zenithar](/wiki/Lore:Zenithar "Lore:Zenithar"), the god of wealth, to bring us some fortune, but thieves made off with my sacred amulet almost as soon as I bought it.*

Volunteering to retrieve the amulet triggers the start of the quest.

| Name | ID | Type | [Weight](/wiki/File:SR-icon-clothing-Leather_Backpack_(square).png "Weight") | [Value](/wiki/File:SR-item-Gold-heads.png "Value") | Enchantment |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Shahvee's Amulet of Zenithar | 000bfa0a | Amulet | 1 | 200 | *Prices are 10% better:*  - [Fortify Barter](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Barter "Skyrim:Fortify Barter"), 10 pts - Disenchant: No |

When you return the amulet, Shahvee gives you a one point bonus in both [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") and [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking"), commenting, "*Before I came into Zenithar's calling, I confess I was a thief. But I learned a few things in my time that might help you survive. Let me show you.*"

## Notes

- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.
- It is impossible to do both quests at the same time, e.g., if you do the quest for Amren, you are unable to do it for Shahvee until you have completed the quest for Amren.
- Shahvee's Amulet can spawn in Uttering Hills Camp, a location that also has a chance for Annekke Crag-Jumper or Brunwulf Free-Winter's personal quests. If they do, none of these quests can be taken at the same time. Waiting 30 days outside their map cells will allow one of the other quests to be taken.

## Bugs

- You may be unable to receive this quest from Shahvee, even if none of the other quests are active.

## Quest Stages

| Dungeon Delving (Bandits) (Favor204) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Find <Alias=QuestItem> inside <Alias=Dungeon> |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Return <Alias=QuestItem> to <Alias.ShortName=QuestGiver> |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor204 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor204`.

# Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)

## Overview

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Fight or sneak your way through a dungeon.
2. Retrieve an item.
3. Return the item.

## Detailed Walkthrough

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from any of the following five people. The dungeon is randomly determined from those in the table, which are based on the hold in which the quest-giver resides.

| Region | Location | Quest Giver | Quest Item | Dialogue Trigger | Reward | Dungeon(s) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"), [Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine") | [Roggi Knot-Beard](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi_Knot-Beard "Skyrim:Roggi Knot-Beard") | [Roggi's Ancestral Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Roggi%27s_Ancestral_Shield "Skyrim:Roggi's Ancestral Shield") | "Are you from Kynesgrove?" | +1 [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") skill increase, plus he'll be available as a follower | [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund"), [Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope"), [Cronvangr Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Hall "Skyrim:Cronvangr Hall"), [Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout"), [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), [Uttering Hills Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Camp "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Camp") |

| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), [The Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle") | [Frida](/wiki/Skyrim:Frida "Skyrim:Frida") | [Ring of Pure Mixtures](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Pure_Mixtures "Skyrim:Ring of Pure Mixtures") | "How'd you pick up the herb trade?" | +1 [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill increase | [Forsaken Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsaken_Cave "Skyrim:Forsaken Cave"), [Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb"), [Shrouded Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Grove "Skyrim:Shrouded Grove") |

## Notes

- Once you've turned in these quests, the items you were meant to retrieve can then be either pickpocketed from the quest-giver, looted off their corpse, or purchased from them if they are a merchant. The most valuable item to take is the Ring of Pure Mixtures, which is one of only two guaranteed [Fortify Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alchemy "Skyrim:Fortify Alchemy") enchantments in the game that can be disenchanted (and the only one that does not require you to join a faction or complete an optional leg of a particular quest). It can be purchased from Frida once you deliver it, but only with the Merchant perk.
- If you make Roggi Knot-Beard a follower, you may be able to take the shield from his inventory.
- Only one radiant quest of a similar type can be assigned at any given time. You must clear the radiant quest from your miscellaneous quests in order to be eligible to receive another of the same type.
- Because this is a favor quest which affects the quest giver's disposition, it will count towards the "Help the People" part of the [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") quest for the quest giver's hold.
- Frida and Oengul will only have the relevant dialogue options during their business hours.

## Bugs

- [Shrouded Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrouded_Grove "Skyrim:Shrouded Grove") should also have been available for Frida's quest, but the location wasn't marked as a cave.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- For the skill-increase rewards, the quest giver may say that they are giving you the training, but the skill does not actually increase, and you don't get a notification that it has increased. **?**

:   - This may happen when that skill was very close to leveling up anyway when you returned the item to the quest giver. One possible solution is to reload a save from before you returned the item, level up that skill by other means (using it, hiring a [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers"), or reading a [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books")), and then turn the item in.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor205 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor205`.

# Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") |
| Location(s): | [Radiant](#Radiant_Options) |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =2 (quest giver) |
| ID: | Favor158 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Thane of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Thane of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Thane of Winterhold") | | |

The Helm of Winterhold

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Obtain quest from [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold").
2. Journey to the target location.
3. Retrieve the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold").
4. Return to Korir with the helm.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When asking the Jarl of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"), [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir"), for work, you may be asked to find the missing [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold"), which was worn by [Jarl Hanse](/wiki/Lore:Jarl_Hanse "Lore:Jarl Hanse") in the First Era:

:   **You're the Jarl? I'm looking for work.**
:   *"Winterhold has lost much of its history, and with that much of its power. I aim to change that. I've heard rumors of the resting place of the Helm of Winterhold, the very same helm that Jarl Hanse wore in the First Era. Hanse was in line to be High King of Skyrim, you know. Having that might get the ear of the other Holds and give me some authority."*

Once you've agreed to find it, head to the location marked on your map, and head to the boss chest, where you will find the helm. The location will be randomly selected from the following: [Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge"), [Fort Fellhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Fellhammer "Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer"), [Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly"), [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave"), [Ironbind Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironbind_Barrow "Skyrim:Ironbind Barrow"), [Pride of Tel Vos](/wiki/Skyrim:Pride_of_Tel_Vos "Skyrim:Pride of Tel Vos"), [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"), [Snow Veil Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Veil_Sanctum "Skyrim:Snow Veil Sanctum"), [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow"), [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild").

After you have retrieved the helm, return to Korir to receive your reward.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 500 |
| 10–19 | 750 |
| 20–29 | 1,000 |
| 30–39 | 1,250 |
| 40+ | 1,500 |

## Notes

- The journal entry for Driftshade Refuge is listed as Driftshade Sanctuary.
- If the location of the helm is at Hela's Folly, you will need to steal the helm from a locked chest. If you are caught by [Deekus](/wiki/Skyrim:Deekus "Skyrim:Deekus"), he will take everything you stole from the chest except the helm. If arrested by a guard, they will also not take the helm, as its status as a quest item supersedes its stolen status.
- You cannot get this quest if Korir is not Jarl of Winterhold. Fortunately, it is only a prerequisite for becoming Thane while Korir is Jarl: if he is replaced, his replacement [Kraldar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kraldar "Skyrim:Kraldar") will give you the title without completing this quest or any other.
- The helm can be pickpocketed back off Korir if you are skilled enough. It will no longer be a quest item, but appears to retain its Stolen status even if sold to a Thieves Guild fence and repurchased (at least, this was the case with Mallus Maccius in Skyrim Special Edition).
- Unlike many "named" objects, there is nothing much special about the Helm of Winterhold. Once it stops being a quest item, it has the exact same properties and sale price as an unenchanted Steel Helmet.
  - As of the latest version of Skyrim Special Edition, this also means it can be tempered with a Steel Ingot and the Steel Smithing perk. It can even be enchanted. The latter is not possible while it is still a quest item.

## Bugs

- If this quest sends you to [Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow"), it breaks [the associated quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol's Barrow"), causing [Yngol's Shade](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Yngol's Shade"), the [Helm of Yngol](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Yngol "Skyrim:Helm of Yngol"), and the skeleton it rests upon not to appear as intended.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- This quest commonly conflicts with [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge"), causing one or the other to be unable to start until the other is completed.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- The quest may, through unknown conditions, become repeatable: pointing you to different locations every time it is given.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- If you have initiated this quest but subsequently went on to finish the [Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim") questline for the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") - or if Winterhold changes hands during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") in the Main Quest line - Korir will be replaced as the jarl and be relocated to [Brunwulf Free-Winter's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). If you try to give him the helm after Brunwulf becomes Jarl of Windhelm, he is continuously locked up in the house, and picking the lock will only result in him telling you you're trespassing. There is no way to finish the quest and you are stuck with the helm in your inventory, as it cannot be dropped since it's a quest item.
  - The quest can be completed by attacking and luring Korir outside, calming him, and then speaking with him before he heads back inside. This will incur a bounty. Trying to engage him in conversation just as you are leaving will also lead to him following you outside.
  -  Alternatively, open up the console, click on the jarl and then type `Addtofaction 0005A1​A4 1` into the box. This adds an NPC to the player ally faction, which will make a normally hostile NPC be non-hostile. This should allow you to complete the quest.
  -  You can also finish the quest by typing `setstage Favor158 20`. This will also remove the helm from your inventory.
- Jarl Korir may not give a dialogue option to start this quest.
  -  Some reports suggest that the quest is flagged as completed as soon as one gains access to the College.
  -  This quest can only be started the first time you visit Winterhold, if you fast travel away before initiating the quest then you won't be able to start it.
  -  Starting the quest via console does not work. You can bypass this quest and still become Thane of Winterhold on PC with `player.setrelationshiprank 1c1b5 2`.

# Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens)

## Overview

*"My father died trying to negotiate with the Forsworn, back when that was possible. They took his shield to those Hagraven beasts they consort with. I need you to bring it home where it belongs."*

## Radiant Options

This is a radiant quest which you can receive from [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

| QuestGiver | QuestGiverHome | QuestItem | Dungeon(s) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") | [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep") ([Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth")) | [Hrolfdir's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrolfdir%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Hrolfdir's Shield") | [Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff"), [Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave"), [Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock"), [Hag's End](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End "Skyrim:Hag's End"), [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt") |

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund").
2. Find Hrolfdir's Shield.
3. Bring Hrolfdir's Shield to Igmund.

## Detailed Walkthrough

When you ask Igmund if he has more work for you, he will mention how his father was killed by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") when he tried to negotiate with them. He will then ask you to retrieve his father's shield, which is being guarded by a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").

Note that [Bleakwind Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Bluff "Skyrim:Bleakwind Bluff") is by far the easiest location from which to retrieve the shield, as it is a small tower with no interior zones and is only inhabited by a few Forsworn and a hagraven. So if you don't feel like doing an extensive dungeon delve, it is expedient to reload until you get that radiant location. Unlike the previous favor, you don't need to kill anyone, so a stealthy character can easily grab the shield and get out without having to fight.

### Reward

As a reward, you will get a leveled piece of armor, which is either a light/heavy cuirass, helmet, or shield of the best quality for your level. In addition, you'll be able to purchase [Vlindrel Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vlindrel_Hall "Skyrim:Vlindrel Hall") from [Raerek](/wiki/Skyrim:Raerek "Skyrim:Raerek"). After completing the quest, the shield can be found in the Jarl's private quarters.

Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Shield "Skyrim:Ebony Shield") | |

[†](#note_1)The list includes results for lower levels, but the quest can only be started at level 20 or higher.

## Notes

- You cannot get this quest if Igmund is not Jarl of Markarth.
  - If you have already started the quest, but Markarth comes under Stormcloak control, you will need to find Igmund in the Blue Palace's basement in order to turn in the quest.
- If you meet all the requirements for the start of this quest but the dialogue with Igmund is not appearing, try visiting the [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrine of Talos") in Markarth before returning to speak with Igmund. The dialogue should then be available.

## Bugs

- If you have accepted but not completed this quest and Markarth comes under Stormcloak control, such that Igmund is no longer the jarl, the quest marker will still point you to Markarth, despite the fact that Igmund is now in exile in the Blue Palace. **?**

## Quest Stages

| Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens) (Favor157) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Find Hrolfdir's Shield for Igmund |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Bring Hrolfdir's Shield to Igmund |
| 20 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage Favor157 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest Favor157`.

# Skyrim:Dungeon Quests

## Overview

The following **side quests** and **miscellaneous quests** generally start when you approach or explore the listed **dungeons** and progress to completion within each dungeon. Each quest is categorized as a dungeon quest in the game data and the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* and usually provides a backstory about the associated dungeon. For information on the many other quests involving dungeons, see the [Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Quests "Skyrim:Quests") page.

## Dungeon Side Quests

-  **[Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darklight+Tower)
  - **[Repentance](/wiki/Skyrim:Repentance "Skyrim:Repentance")**: Help [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") prevent her mother [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") from transforming into a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").
-  **[Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dragon Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cultist "Skyrim:Dragon Cultist"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forelhost)
  - **[Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult")**: Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") to recover his mask for [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir").
-  **[Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and the unique wispmother the [Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady_(creature) "Skyrim:The Pale Lady (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostmere+Crypt)
  - **[The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")**: Find out what happened in [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt").
-  **[High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Gate+Ruins)
  - **[A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska")**: Help [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") trace her roots in [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins").
-  **[Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hillgrund%27s+Tomb)
  - **[Ancestral Worship](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestral_Worship "Skyrim:Ancestral Worship")**: Help [Golldir](/wiki/Skyrim:Golldir "Skyrim:Golldir") save his [aunt](/wiki/Skyrim:Agna "Skyrim:Agna") and stop a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vals_Veran "Skyrim:Vals Veran") from defiling his [ancestral barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb").
- **[Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") accessed from inside [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nchuand-Zel)
  - **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").
-  **[Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Treva%27s+Watch)
  - **[Infiltration](/wiki/Skyrim:Infiltration "Skyrim:Infiltration")**: Help [Stalleo](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalleo "Skyrim:Stalleo") take back [Treva's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Treva%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Treva's Watch").
-  **[Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Valthume)
  - **[Evil in Waiting](/wiki/Skyrim:Evil_in_Waiting "Skyrim:Evil in Waiting")**: Seal away an [ancient evil](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(creature) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (creature)").
-  **[Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the ghost of [Kvenel the Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Kvenel_the_Tongue "Skyrim:Kvenel the Tongue"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Volunruud)
  - **[Silenced Tongues](/wiki/Skyrim:Silenced_Tongues "Skyrim:Silenced Tongues")**: Unlock the burial chamber of the Tongue Chieftain [Kvenel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kvenel_the_Tongue "Skyrim:Kvenel the Tongue").

## Dungeon Miscellaneous Quests

-  **[Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Angarvunde)
  - **[Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde_(quest) "Skyrim:Angarvunde (quest)")**: Discover the treasure of [Angarvunde](/wiki/Skyrim:Angarvunde "Skyrim:Angarvunde").
-  **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") led by [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ansilvund)
  - **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").
-  **[Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") along the banks of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
  - **[The Affairs of Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Affairs_of_Hagravens "Skyrim:The Affairs of Hagravens")**: After discovering an [imprisoned hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Melka "Skyrim:Melka"), you must help her reclaim her lost tower.
-  **[Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse")** — A lighthouse west-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostflow+Lighthouse)
  - **[Frostflow Abyss](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Abyss "Skyrim:Frostflow Abyss")**: Uncover the tragic events inside [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").
-  **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing the [Mistwatch Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit") and their [leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistwatch)
  - **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)")**: Help [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") locate his kidnapped wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola").
-  **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern")** — A small, open-roofed [cavernous](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") grove lush with many kinds of flora and fungi, located due north of [Hunter's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hunter's Rest") and northwest of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill") which is inhabited by bears and spriggans. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moss+Mother+Cavern)
  - **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)")**: Help an [injured hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") avenge his fallen companions.
-  **[Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim")** — A small ruined [Nordic tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Towers "Skyrim:Nordic Towers") east-northeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") disguised as guards. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nilheim)
  - **[Telrav's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav%27s_Request "Skyrim:Telrav's Request")**: Escort [Telrav](/wiki/Skyrim:Telrav "Skyrim:Telrav") back to his camp in [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim").
-  **[Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Otar the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar_the_Mad "Skyrim:Otar the Mad"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ragnvald)
  - **[Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald_(quest) "Skyrim:Ragnvald (quest)")**: Discover the secrets of [Ragnvald](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragnvald "Skyrim:Ragnvald").
-  **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rebel%27s+Cairn)
  - **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")**: Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").
-  **[Sleeping Tree Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sleeping+Tree+Camp)
  - **[Sleeping Tree Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave_(quest) "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave (quest)")**: Question [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") about an interesting [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_Message "Skyrim:Ysolda's Message") you found on a [dead Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag").
-  **[Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing the conjurer [Bashnag](/wiki/Skyrim:Bashnag "Skyrim:Bashnag") and his [coven](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellsword_(NPC) "Skyrim:Spellsword (NPC)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Southfringe+Sanctum)
  - **[The Savior of Selveni Nethri](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Savior_of_Selveni_Nethri "Skyrim:The Savior of Selveni Nethri")**: Help a necromancer escape from [Southfringe Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Southfringe_Sanctum "Skyrim:Southfringe Sanctum").
-  **[Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing the [shade](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Yngol's Shade") of an ancient Nord warrior. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Yngol+Barrow)
  - **[Yngol's Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol's Barrow")**: Find the treasure unlocked by the [Coral Dragon Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Coral_Dragon_Claw "Skyrim:Coral Dragon Claw").

# Skyrim:Dungeon Quests

## Overview

The following **side quests** and **miscellaneous quests** generally start when you approach or explore the listed **dungeons** and progress to completion within each dungeon. Each quest is categorized as a dungeon quest in the game data and the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* and usually provides a backstory about the associated dungeon. For information on the many other quests involving dungeons, see the [Quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Quests "Skyrim:Quests") page.

## Dungeon Side Quests

-  **[Darklight Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Darklight_Tower "Skyrim:Darklight Tower")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darklight+Tower)
  - **[Repentance](/wiki/Skyrim:Repentance "Skyrim:Repentance")**: Help [Illia](/wiki/Skyrim:Illia "Skyrim:Illia") prevent her mother [Silvia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silvia "Skyrim:Silvia") from transforming into a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven").
-  **[Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [Dragon Cultists](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Cultist "Skyrim:Dragon Cultist"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forelhost)
  - **[Siege on the Dragon Cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Siege_on_the_Dragon_Cult "Skyrim:Siege on the Dragon Cult")**: Enter the ruins of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost") and defeat [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(creature) "Skyrim:Rahgot (creature)") to recover his mask for [Captain Valmir](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Valmir "Skyrim:Captain Valmir").
-  **[Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and the unique wispmother the [Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady_(creature) "Skyrim:The Pale Lady (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostmere+Crypt)
  - **[The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")**: Find out what happened in [Frostmere Crypt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostmere_Crypt "Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt").
-  **[High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(creature) "Skyrim:Vokun (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=High+Gate+Ruins)
  - **[A Scroll For Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Scroll_For_Anska "Skyrim:A Scroll For Anska")**: Help [Anska](/wiki/Skyrim:Anska "Skyrim:Anska") trace her roots in [High Gate Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Gate_Ruins "Skyrim:High Gate Ruins").
-  **[Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hillgrund%27s+Tomb)

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Volunruud)

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ansilvund)

-  **[Blind Cliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Blind_Cliff_Cave "Skyrim:Blind Cliff Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") along the banks of the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blind+Cliff+Cave)
  - **[The Affairs of Hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Affairs_of_Hagravens "Skyrim:The Affairs of Hagravens")**: After discovering an [imprisoned hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Melka "Skyrim:Melka"), you must help her reclaim her lost tower.
-  **[Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse")** — A lighthouse west-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostflow+Lighthouse)
  - **[Frostflow Abyss](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Abyss "Skyrim:Frostflow Abyss")**: Uncover the tragic events inside [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").
-  **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing the [Mistwatch Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit") and their [leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistwatch)
  - **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_(quest) "Skyrim:Mistwatch (quest)")**: Help [Christer](/wiki/Skyrim:Christer "Skyrim:Christer") locate his kidnapped wife [Fjola](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjola "Skyrim:Fjola").
-  **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern")** — A small, open-roofed [cavernous](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") grove lush with many kinds of flora and fungi, located due north of [Hunter's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hunter's Rest") and northwest of [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill") which is inhabited by bears and spriggans. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Moss+Mother+Cavern)
  - **[Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern_(quest) "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern (quest)")**: Help an [injured hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Valdr "Skyrim:Valdr") avenge his fallen companions.

  - **[Rebel's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebel%27s_Cairn_(quest) "Skyrim:Rebel's Cairn (quest)")**: Find [Red Eagle's](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle "Skyrim:Red Eagle") [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Red Eagle's Bane").
-  **[Sleeping Tree Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sleeping+Tree+Camp)
  - **[Sleeping Tree Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Cave_(quest) "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Cave (quest)")**: Question [Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda") about an interesting [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda%27s_Message "Skyrim:Ysolda's Message") you found on a [dead Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulag "Skyrim:Ulag").

[(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Southfringe+Sanctum)

-  **[Yngol Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol_Barrow "Skyrim:Yngol Barrow")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") northeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing the [shade](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngol%27s_Shade "Skyrim:Yngol's Shade") of an ancient Nord warrior.
