# Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins

## Overview

Mzulft, a large Dwarven ruin

 This page lists all the **Dwarven ruins** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

:    **[Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand")** — A large Dwarven ruin southwest of Winterhold containing Dwarven automatons, Falmer, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Alftand)
:    **[Arkngthamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Arkngthamz "Skyrim:Arkngthamz")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small Dwarven ruin southeast of Dushnikh Yal containing Dwarven automatons, Falmer, and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Arkngthamz+%28DG%29)
:    **[Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel")** — A medium-sized Dwarven ruin west of Riften containing Dwarven automatons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Avanchnzel)
:   **[Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach")** — An immense, naturally lit cavern inhabited by hordes of Falmer and containing the ruins of a Dwemer city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blackreach)

    :   **[Debate Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Debate_Hall "Skyrim:Debate Hall")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer and their servants.
    :   **[Derelict Pumphouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Derelict_Pumphouse "Skyrim:Derelict Pumphouse")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by a Dwarven spider.
    :   **[Farm Overseer's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Farm_Overseer%27s_House "Skyrim:Farm Overseer's House")** — A small Dwarven building in Blackreach.
    :   **[Hall of Rumination](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Rumination "Skyrim:Hall of Rumination")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer and their servants.
    :   **[Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer servants.
    :   **[Reeking Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Reeking_Tower "Skyrim:Reeking Tower")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by frostbite spiders.
    :   **[Silent City Catacombs](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_City_Catacombs "Skyrim:Silent City Catacombs")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach occupied by Falmer.
    :   **[Silent Ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Silent_Ruin "Skyrim:Silent Ruin")** — A small Dwarven ruin in Blackreach.
    :   **[Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory")** — A small Dwarven building in Blackreach serving as Sinderion's alchemical foothold in the cavern.
    :   **[War Quarters](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Quarters "Skyrim:War Quarters")** — A small Dwarven building in Blackreach.
:    **[Bthardamz](/wiki/Skyrim:Bthardamz "Skyrim:Bthardamz")** — A large Dwarven ruin west-northwest of Karthwasten containing Afflicted and Dwarven automatons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bthardamz)
:    **[Deep Folk Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Deep_Folk_Crossing "Skyrim:Deep Folk Crossing")** — An ancient Dwarven bridge over a weir with structures at either end in the northern part of the Reach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Deep+Folk+Crossing)
:    **[Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large Dwarven ruin east of the Water Stone containing rieklings, albino spiders, oil spiders, and Dwarven automatons. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Fahlbtharz)
:    **[Great Lift at Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Alftand "Skyrim:Great Lift at Alftand")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located northeast of Nightgate Inn and southeast of Wayward Pass. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Alftand)
:    **[Great Lift at Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Great Lift at Mzinchaleft")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located south of Mzinchaleft. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Mzinchaleft)
:    **[Great Lift at Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Great_Lift_at_Raldbthar "Skyrim:Great Lift at Raldbthar")** — A Dwarven lift to Blackreach located west-southwest of Anga's Mill and east of Irkngthand. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Raldbthar)
:    **[Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand")** — A large Dwarven ruin west of Windhelm containing bandits, Dwarven automatons, Falmer, frostbite spiders, and skeevers. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Irkngthand)
:    **[Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel")** — A small Dwarven ruin southeast of Windhelm containing Falmer. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kagrenzel)
:    **[Kagrumez](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrumez "Skyrim:Kagrumez")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A small Dwarven ruin south of the Temple of Miraak. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Kagrumez)
:    **[Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft")** — A medium-sized Dwarven ruin southwest of Dawnstar containing bandits, Dwarven automatons, Falmer, and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzinchaleft)
:    **[Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft")** — A large Dwarven ruin south-southeast of Windhelm containing Dwarven automatons, Falmer, and chaurus. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzulft)
:    **[Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") — A large Dwarven ruin north-northeast of Tel Mithryn. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Nchardak)
:   **[Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel")** — A large Dwarven ruin accessed from inside Understone Keep. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nchuand-Zel)
:    **[Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar")** — A medium-sized Dwarven ruin west-southwest of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Raldbthar)
:    **[Reachwind Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachwind_Eyrie "Skyrim:Reachwind Eyrie")** — A small Dwarven tower east-southeast of Markarth. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Reachwind+Eyrie)
:    **[Ruins of Bthalft](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Bthalft "Skyrim:Ruins of Bthalft")** — A small Dwarven ruin south of Ivarstead containing bandits. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Bthalft)
:    **[Ruins of Rkund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Rkund "Skyrim:Ruins of Rkund")** — A small Dwarven ruin in the mountains southwest of Riften containing a wispmother and wisps. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ruins+of+Rkund)
:    **[Tower of Mzark](/wiki/Skyrim:Tower_of_Mzark "Skyrim:Tower of Mzark")** — A small Dwarven tower in Blackreach. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tower+of+Mzark)

# Skyrim:Earth Stone

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Standing Stones.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Standing_Stones.png) | All-Maker Stone: Earth Stone ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Earth+Stone)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2StoneEarth, DLC2StoneEarth02, DLC2RavenRock05 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| Southwest of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") Northwest of [Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm") | |

The Earth Stone

The **Earth Stone** is an [All-Maker Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones") southwest of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

Once [cleansed](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones"), this stone gives you the power to [ignore](/wiki/Skyrim:Bones_of_the_Earth "Skyrim:Bones of the Earth") 80% of all physical damage for 30 seconds. This power is essentially identical to the master-level [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") spell [Dragonhide](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonhide "Skyrim:Dragonhide"), though without the casting delay, high magicka cost, or skill requirement. Once you use this power, it disappears from the Powers menu, and you must return to the Earth Stone to obtain it again.

## Related Quests

- **[Cleansing the Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones")**: Use the [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") to cleanse each of the remaining [All-Maker Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones").

## Walkthrough

The cleansed Earth Stone

The stone shows the usual signs of construction, with wooden scaffolding on the southeast side, and [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), [shovels](/wiki/Skyrim:Shovel "Skyrim:Shovel"), hammers, and carts in the vicinity. Several [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") and [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants grow around the stone. A path leads northeast to Raven Rock, which is nearby.

Before you cleanse the stone, if [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)") has not been completed, [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") will speak to you as you approach. During the day, [Bralsa Drel](/wiki/Skyrim:Bralsa_Drel "Skyrim:Bralsa Drel"), [Rirns Llervu](/wiki/Skyrim:Rirns_Llervu "Skyrim:Rirns Llervu"), and three [Redoran guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") will be working on and bowing to the stone. During the night, [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano"), [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor"), [Garyn Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Garyn_Ienth "Skyrim:Garyn Ienth"), [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory"), and [Milore Ienth](/wiki/Skyrim:Milore_Ienth "Skyrim:Milore Ienth") will also be found at the stone. When you cleanse the stone, a leveled [lurker](/wiki/Skyrim:Lurker "Skyrim:Lurker") will rise from the water around the base of the stone and attack you and the workers, followed by a second leveled lurker approaching from the coast to the west; the Redoran guards will aid in the fight. After the lurkers are defeated, the workers will express their thanks and return to Raven Rock.

## Notes

- The Earth Stone also appears in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Earth_Stone "Bloodmoon:Earth Stone")*, when it was northwest of Raven Rock, not southwest.

# Skyrim:East Empire Company (place)

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: East Empire Company ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=East+Empire+Company)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company")) | | |

| Console Location Code(s) | |

| Location | |
| [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") | |

.jpg)

East Empire Company

The **East Empire Company** is the regional office for the [company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") on the docks of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). The office is almost completely bare and run down before completing the relevant quest. It is located between the [Clan Shatter-Shield Office](/wiki/Skyrim:Clan_Shatter-Shield_Office "Skyrim:Clan Shatter-Shield Office") and the western end of the docks.

Before Rise in the East is complete

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Orthus Endario](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthus_Endario "Skyrim:Orthus Endario")  [Adelaisa Vendicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adelaisa_Vendicci "Skyrim:Adelaisa Vendicci")\* [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") |

\* This person only appears once you return from [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") with information during the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East") for Orthus.

## Related Quests

- **[The Arms of Chaos](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:The Arms of Chaos")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Arms_of_Chaos "Skyrim:Arms of Chaos"): Complete a mage's quest to reassemble two powerful staves.
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

## East Empire Company

Afterwards

When you first visit the office, it is dark, dusty, and full of cobwebs. There are round wooden tables in alcoves to the east and west, with the latter holding the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") and a level-locked non-respawning [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") containing random items on top. There is a partition wall splitting the building into two rooms, with a doorway in the middle joining them. The rest of the office contains a few crates and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sacks, but not much else, except empty shelves.

After completing the quest [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East"), the office and company will be restored. Once restored, the office is fairly well lit, clean, and tidy. There are still crates, barrels, and sacks of foodstuffs all around both rooms. There is a set of shelves to the left of the doorway holding a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"), a [philter of the defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Philter_of_the_Defender "Skyrim:Philter of the Defender"), a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the right of the doorway is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a bottle of wine and a bottle of Nord mead on top. To the east, against the wall is a long wooden table holding a [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") and a bottle of Nord mead. Through the doorway into the second room, there is a set of shelves holding copies of *[Brief History of the Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire")* (the complete series), *[Report: Disaster at Ionith](/wiki/Skyrim:Report:_Disaster_at_Ionith "Skyrim:Report: Disaster at Ionith")*, *[Mixed Unit Tactics](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixed_Unit_Tactics "Skyrim:Mixed Unit Tactics")*, *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*, *[The Cake and The Diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cake_and_The_Diamond "Skyrim:The Cake and The Diamond")*, and *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*. In the northeastern corner, on a crate is a bottle of alto wine, and in the southeastern corner, in a bucket on the floor is a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").

## Notes

- The dressers in the location are non-respawning.

## Bugs

- Orthus Endario and Adelaisa Vendicci have sleep packages here, but the building has no beds for them.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse

## Overview

East Empire Company Warehouse

The **East Empire Company Warehouse** is a warehouse on the [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") docks immediately southeast of the city.

Warehouse interior

The building is the headquarters and main warehouse for the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). Normally, the entrance is locked with a leveled lock, and you will be considered to be trespassing if you enter. There is usually a [Solitude guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard") patrolling just outside the entrance, while the interior of the warehouse is occupied by [Dockworkers](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Dockworker "Skyrim:East Empire Dockworker"), the [Dockmaster](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Dockmaster "Skyrim:East Empire Dockmaster"), and [Snorreid](/wiki/Skyrim:Snorreid "Skyrim:Snorreid"), as well as a complement of three patrolling Solitude guards. When the quest [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly") is started, the Solitude guards, Dockworkers, and Dockmaster are replaced by [wardens](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Warden "Skyrim:East Empire Warden"), who are hostile to all trespassers.

Inside the warehouse is an entrance to [Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto"), which has a second (exterior) entrance near the [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse"). There is a large amount of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), [clothing](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") in the warehouse, as listed below.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Snorreid](/wiki/Skyrim:Snorreid "Skyrim:Snorreid")  [East Empire Wardens](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Warden "Skyrim:East Empire Warden") \* |

\* They replace the [Dockmaster](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Dockmaster "Skyrim:East Empire Dockmaster"), [Dockworkers](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Dockworker "Skyrim:East Empire Dockworker"), and three [Solitude guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard "Skyrim:Solitude Guard") during the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").
- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.

### Exterior

The area outside has a small structure on your left containing 20 [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), a [knife weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(weapon) "Skyrim:Knife (weapon)"), and a copy of *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_Prince "Skyrim:Beggar Prince")*. You'll find an unlocked chest and a barrel underwater. On the other side of the dock, three harvestable [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), a bucket, a fishing rod, and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on a barrel await you. [Jolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Jolf "Skyrim:Jolf") sits near a ferry on your left. The path on your right leads to the [Red Wave](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave").

### East Empire Company Warehouse

East Empire Company Sign

The entrance leads into a shack-like structure, with a table on your right holding a piece of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"); a warden/Solitude guard will be here, with another patrolling the passageway just ahead. The inside of the warehouse consists of indoor docks, with berths on both sides of the building and the waterway between them. There is a path along the waterside leading past stacks of crates bearing the East Empire Company crest, and another shack containing nothing but an empty table. There are shelves throughout the zone filled with all manner of items, including crates, bales of straw, sawn logs, furniture, food barrels, and many other items. The shelves form passages between them. Near the start of the shelves, you can climb a ramp to the top of a shelf with an entire rib cage of a mammoth ahead. You can then climb a split log to the left and jump across to another shelf opposite, where there are several crates and an end table holding a copy of [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Buying Game](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Buying_Game "Skyrim:The Buying Game")*. There is a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") ahead across another gap, and above the urn on a shelf is a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest").

Continuing through the passage between the shelves on the lower level, after you pass a pile of carriage wheels, ahead and to the right is a flight of wooden stairs leading down into the water. Around the corner, near several unusable anvils and a selection of [steel, iron and silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots"), is a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill book *[Heavy Armor Forging](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_Forging "Skyrim:Heavy Armor Forging")*. Just past this area is a master-locked gate, but there is nothing in the area behind it. To the right of the gate is a flight of stairs leading up, with a novice-locked chest on the ground behind it. At the top there are more stairs leading up, and at the very top you will find [Snorreid](/wiki/Skyrim:Snorreid "Skyrim:Snorreid") either sleeping on one of three bed rolls or sitting at a table eating. There are more shelves here holding many food barrels, dressers of random clothes, and an apprentice-locked chest. Returning to the lower level, there is a warden (or dockworker, depending if you are here during the Guild quest or not) guarding the first docked boat, which has an apprentice-locked chest on board. There is a rowboat on top of one of the shelves, and an adept-locked chest on the ground beneath it. Just after this is a boat that has been raised out of the water for repairs, with stairs up on this side; six bowls of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat") appear to be being used to waterproof the boat and deck. Another warden/dockworker patrols around this boat, with a fourth on the far side who is often within earshot. Beyond the boat under repair are more shelves, with wide stairs leading up at the end of the shelves. Just beyond the stairs up are stairs leading down into the water. Beyond these stairs are more shelves, with a tall ladder leaning against them. You are able to climb the ladder to the third shelf, where there is a novice-locked chest. Next to these shelves is another flight of stairs down into the water, and more shelves continue to the end by the large sea doors. At the very end is a table with the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on top. A guard/warden patrols this walkway.

Returning to the stairs leading up, at the top are more shelves, with two life-sized statues to [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella") on the top shelf that you cannot interact with. Past these statues, the path climbs steeply to the Dockmaster's cabin, which has double wooden doors that are kept unlocked. The cabin is in a poor state of repair, with large holes in the walls and roof. Inside is a long wooden table against the southwestern wall with the [East Empire Shipping Map](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Shipping_Map "Skyrim:East Empire Shipping Map"), a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), nineteen loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), a [silver amethyst ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Amethyst_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Amethyst Ring"), a [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Ring"), and a leveled [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring "Skyrim:Ring"). The map can be sold to [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") as part of the quest [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny"). A dresser to the left of the table holds a selection of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), and has a [wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt") on top. There is an unowned single bed opposite the entrance, with a medium coin purse on the floor by its foot, and a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast") on the floor beside it. A small round table to the right of the bed holds a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). There are two bunches of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam") and a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") hanging from the rafters, and against the northeastern wall is a cupboard and a set of shelves that hold five bottles of alto wine, four bottles of wine, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), and twelve common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"). To the right of the shelves is a bucket containing another gourd.

Back at the bottom, descend the stairs into the water near the ones you've just climbed, then turn north at the wall to climb a short wooden ramp. This is a dead end until you arrive here during the related quest, at which time you may pass between the shelves to reach a concealed entrance to the main section of Brinewater Grotto.

These are all the items found either on or under the large multi-leveled shelves throughout the warehouse:

- 10 [Goat Cheese Wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel")
- 2 [Sliced Goat Cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese")
- 23 [Eidar Cheese Wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel")
- 14 Gourds
- 5 Dried Elves Ear
- 8 [Cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage")
- 3 [Horker Meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat")
- 1 [Cow Hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide")
- 1 [Cave Bear Pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt")
- 1 Wolf Pelt

‡ These are in addition to those being used to repair the ship.

## Notes

- There is a  "Danger") Danger [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowmarks_(Thieves_Guild) "Skyrim:Shadowmarks (Thieves Guild)") to the right of the entrance door. This is due to the quest Scoundrel's Folly, when the workers are replaced by hostile wardens.
- The Warehouse's items respawn, and will prove useful to anyone in need of minor potions, troll fat, [giant's toes](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), [food and drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), [iron weaponry](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron#Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron"), and general clutter.
- This is the only location in the game where you can find two fixed sets of noble clothes.
- Under the water is a single unlocked chest containing only minor loot. It is just to the south of the berthed boat.
- Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the wine bottles in the small structure outside the building as owned by the Warehouse.

## Bugs

- There are two pairs of boots you cannot interact with unless you knock them back into bounds. This can be done by standing in that corner and using The Ritual Stone power and possibly by casting certain spells such as fireball at that corner.
- The guard who patrols the dock outside the Warehouse may be found swimming in the water, making it impossible to speak to him. **?**
- There is a Horse Hide amongst the animal pelts that you may not be able to interact with. **?**
- There is a goat which wanders the inside of the warehouse, and a Master-locked empty cage built into one of the shelves. It's likely that the goat was meant to be behind the cage, but spawns instead outside of it. **?**

Dockmaster

The **East Empire Dockmaster** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") found in the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"). He loiters around the warehouse all the time, eating and sleeping at random times.

He wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothes"), along with some [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots") and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#0004223b "Skyrim:Hat"). He carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Dialogue

The Dockmaster will simply greet you with:

:   *"Good day to you."*
:   *"Do you have business with the East Empire Company?"*
:   *"I will thank you not to interrupt me in my tasks."*

## Notes

- Similar to his [dockworkers](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Dockworker "Skyrim:East Empire Dockworker"), he does not get named in-game, although his ref bears the name **Regulus Naevius**, implying he was once meant to be named.
- It seems that the Dockmaster was at one point intended to be a backup for [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici")'s role as East Empire Company vendor. The `DialogueSolitude` quest has an alias denoting him as such, but he has no other traces that this was ever followed up on, as he has no relevant factions, AI, or anything else. He also has the same lines as Vittoria, recorded in his voice type, for use in two scenes involving her that were meant to play at the Solitude docks, which he never goes to.

Nord Dockworker

The **East Empire Dockworkers** are employees found at the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse"). The [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") dockworker wears farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#000209a6 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000209a5 "Skyrim:Boots"). The [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") dockworker wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"). Neither of the dockworkers carry anything in their inventory.

## Notes

- The dockworkers are replaced by [East Empire wardens](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Warden "Skyrim:East Empire Warden") when the quest [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly") is started.
- Both of the dockworkers are members of the [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") class, which determines the level of their skills.
- The Breton dockworker does not have a voice type.
- According to their respective refs, the Nord dockworker's name is **Slading** and the Breton's is **Jonne**.
- Neither of the dockworkers have any AI packages, resulting in them just standing in place unless provoked.

# Skyrim:East Empire Mercenary

## Overview

An East Empire Mercenary

**East Empire Mercenaries** are the four [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Soldier_(class) "Skyrim:Soldier (class)") found on the ship you take to [Japhet's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Japhet%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Japhet's Folly") during the quest [Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East"). After you have helped [Orthus Endario](/wiki/Skyrim:Orthus_Endario "Skyrim:Orthus Endario") by finding information on pirate attacks which have affected the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company")'s business, you'll be approached by [Adelaisa Vendicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adelaisa_Vendicci "Skyrim:Adelaisa Vendicci"), the captain of the East Empire mercenaries. She will request that you accompany the crew to Japhet's Folly to help defeat the pirates.

## Related Quests

- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

### Rise in the East

When you come to the docks for the voyage, one of the East Empire mercenaries will ask you:

:   *"You're the one who's coming to Japhet's Folly with us, right? You ready to go?"*

:   :   **Let's go.**
    :   *"All aboard!"*

:   :   **Not just yet.**
    :   *"Well, hurry it up!"*

East Empire Warden

The **East Empire Wardens** take over the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") during [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly"). The wardens turn hostile if they spot you.

Each warden wears [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots"), and an open-faced [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet"). They carry a leveled [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch"), two leveled [health potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions#Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potions"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a [small amount](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.
- **[When the Cat's Away](/wiki/Skyrim:When_the_Cat%27s_Away "Skyrim:When the Cat's Away")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Silver "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Silver"): Find a stash of [silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver "Skyrim:Silver") armor.

Eastmarch Imperial Camp

**Eastmarch Imperial Camp** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), located southeast of [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft") and north of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave").

Eastmarch Imperial Camp

The camp is normally commanded by [Legate Hrollod](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Hrollod "Skyrim:Legate Hrollod"), except during [The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol"), at which point [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") will assume command until the [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") is initiated.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol")**: Prepare for the final assault on [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") by taking [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!
- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Eastmarch Imperial Camp

It is a very small and compact Imperial camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. To the west is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). To the northeast is the command tent, containing an end table and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the Legate spends most of their time. To the left of the command tent is the Legate's tent, containing an owned single bed, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and an end table beside it. To the left, forming the northwest side of the camp, are three small tents containing unowned bed rolls. To the left of the tents is the hospital tent, which contains three bed rolls occupied by three wounded soldiers and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Outside is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). To the southwest is the quartermaster's tent, in front of which is the workstation for the [Imperial quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Imperial Quartermaster"), consisting of a long wooden table between an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil") on the left, a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") on the right, and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") to the left of the tent. On the table and inside the tent are various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). Farther to the east are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing.

Any time [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") is controlled by the Imperials, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Notes

- After receiving orders for the Battle for Windhelm, the camp will be removed.
- The camp [reappears](/wiki/Legends:Eastmarch_Camp "Legends:Eastmarch Camp") in *[Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends")*.

## Bugs

- If you travel to the site after the camp is struck, NPCs may remain, and objects may be found seemingly floating in midair.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- If you move between the commander's office and the smithing station, the music and weather may randomly change abruptly. **?**

| Eastern [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") | |

A view of Eastmarch, looking southwest from [Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp")

**Eastmarch** is a [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in eastern [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"), with its capital in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). The hold is the home of [Jarl Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak"), leader of the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") rebellion. It only becomes Imperial-run if the player joins the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and completes the entire quest line, including both [the Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol") and the [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm"). Should this occur, the new Jarl will be [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter").

Eastmarch is in the northeastern corner of Skyrim. [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") is to the northwest, [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") and [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") to the west, the [Throat of the World](/wiki/Skyrim:Throat_of_the_World "Skyrim:Throat of the World") to the southwest, and [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") to the south. The [Dunmer](/wiki/Lore:Dunmer "Lore:Dunmer") homeland of [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") is to the east, across the [Velothi Mountain](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains") passes. Since the [Red Year](/wiki/Lore:Red_Year "Lore:Red Year"), Dunmer have had a much bigger presence in Eastmarch, particularly in the capital, due to its proximity to one of the only [passes](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") through the Velothi.

Map of Eastmarch

Windhelm, the hold capital

## Topographical Overview

Bonestrewn Crest rises from the sulfur pools

Eastmarch varies greatly. The central and southern parts of Eastmarch are dominated by sulfurous pools and rocky crags, as well as [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest"). The Velothi Mountains form a spine along the eastern edge of the hold, and a high ridge to the south leads up from the lowland sulfur pools to the Rift.

The [Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River") joins the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") in the west, after which the White River merges with [River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim") at the Windhelm bridge and flows out into the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts").

### Flora and Fauna

The sulfur pools are home to [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"), [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer"), [sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Sabre Cat"), and other, smaller creatures, such as [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") and [goats](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"). Further north are snowy sabre cats, [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"), and [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") along the road to Morrowind.

There are a few [farms](/wiki/Skyrim:Farms "Skyrim:Farms") near Windhelm, but otherwise the only plant in the snowy parts of Eastmarch is the humble [snowberry bush](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"). In the sulfur region to the south, in the middle of the hold, the endemic plants of [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), [Jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), and [creep clusters](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster") are to be found. The pine forest and shrublands surrounding the sulfur region are home to [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), and all common varieties of [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Mountain Flower"). [Mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") and to some extent [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") can also be found throughout the hold. In the last parts of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), stretching from [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill") to the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"), [nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") is common.

### Routes and Pathways

Two main routes run north to south in Eastmarch. They skirt the sulfur pools on either side. The roads are connected to each other at the far northern and southern ends, forming a continuous loop. There are also major branches off of this road: one west of [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol") leading to Whiterun; one west-northwest of [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") leading south to the Rift, and two near Windhelm. One leads to the Pale and beyond, and the other along the Sea of Ghosts past farms until you hit the impassable, invisible wall near [Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest").

There are two pathways into the sulfur pools from the east road: one runs from south of Kynesgrove to [Witchmist Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchmist_Grove "Skyrim:Witchmist Grove"), and the other starts near [Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp") and heads west to Bonestrewn Crest. Other pathways in the hold are to landmarks such as the [dragon mound](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mound "Skyrim:Dragon Mound") above Kynesgrove (and, by extension, [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur")), or [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch").

## Places

All locations in Eastmarch with individual map markers are listed. There are a few places without map markers listed for your convenience.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm")** — A major city in the northeast of Skyrim near the [Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass") to [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind"), and the capital of Eastmarch. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm)
-  **[Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings")** — A large [castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") at the far end of the Valunstrad district in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Palace+of+the+Kings)
-  **[Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables")** — A [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") outside of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm+Stables)

### Farms, Towns, and Settlements including Orc Strongholds and Inns

-  **[Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm")** — A [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") farm, a short distance east of [Windhelm Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Stables "Skyrim:Windhelm Stables"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brandy-Mug+Farm)
-  **[Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing")** — A small mining [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+Crossing)
-  **[Hlaalu Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hlaalu_Farm "Skyrim:Hlaalu Farm")** — A small farm east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hlaalu+Farm)
-  **[Hollyfrost Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Hollyfrost_Farm "Skyrim:Hollyfrost Farm")** — A large farm with a single-roomed farmhouse east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hollyfrost+Farm)
-  **[Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove")** — A small [settlement](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kynesgrove)
-  **[Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill")** — A [lumber mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Mills "Skyrim:Wood Mills") on the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and southeast of [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mixwater+Mill)
-  **[Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur")** — An [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") in the east of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Narzulbur)
-  **[Riverside Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverside_Shack "Skyrim:Riverside Shack")** — A small shack east of [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") and west-southwest of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"), along the eastern bank of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Riverside+Shack)
-  **[Traitor's Post](/wiki/Skyrim:Traitor%27s_Post "Skyrim:Traitor's Post")** — A crumbling [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") and [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") outpost east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), and just north of the [Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Traitor%27s+Post)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Broken Limb Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Limb_Camp "Skyrim:Broken Limb Camp")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") north-northwest of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Limb+Camp)
-  **[Cradlecrush Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradlecrush_Rock "Skyrim:Cradlecrush Rock")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cradlecrush+Rock)
-  **[Eastmarch Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Eastmarch Imperial Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") in Eastmarch, located southeast of [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft") and north of [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eastmarch+Imperial+Camp)
-  **[Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp")** — A [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") south of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steamcrag+Camp)
-  **[Windhelm Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Windhelm Military Camp")** — An [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Camps "Skyrim:Imperial Camps") set up east of [Brandy-Mug Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandy-Mug_Farm "Skyrim:Brandy-Mug Farm") for the [attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") on [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Windhelm+Military+Camp)

### Caves

-  **[Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Shor's Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Shor%27s_Stone "Skyrim:Shor's Stone") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and [pit wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Pit_Wolf "Skyrim:Pit Wolf"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cragslane+Cavern)
-  **[Cragwallow Slope](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragwallow_Slope "Skyrim:Cragwallow Slope")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") home to [conjurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") and [atronachs](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cragwallow+Slope)
-  **[Cronvangr Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Cave "Skyrim:Cronvangr Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cronvangr+Cave)
-  **[Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary")** — A small [underground grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") and worship site of the followers of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth") south-southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Eldergleam+Sanctuary)
-  **[Frostroot Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostroot_Cave "Skyrim:Frostroot Cave")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz:_Dwarven_Home "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home") — A cave in Eastmarch, north of [Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostroot+Cave+%28CC%29)
-  **[Lost Knife Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Knife_Hideout "Skyrim:Lost Knife Hideout")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Knife+Hideout)
- **[Mara's Eye Den](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Den "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Den")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mara%27s+Eye+Den)
-  **[Snapleg Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Snapleg_Cave "Skyrim:Snapleg Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Rift Watchtower](/wiki/Skyrim:Rift_Watchtower "Skyrim:Rift Watchtower") occupied by [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") and [monsters](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters "Skyrim:Monsters"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Snapleg+Cave)
-  **[Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stony+Creek+Cave)
-  **[Uttering Hills Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Uttering_Hills_Cave "Skyrim:Uttering Hills Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Uttering+Hills+Cave)

### Mines

-  **[Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine")** — A small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") supporting the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gloombound+Mine)
- **[Goldenrock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenrock_Mine "Skyrim:Goldenrock Mine")** — A small [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in southeastern [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Goldenrock+Mine)
- **[Steamscorch Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamscorch_Mine "Skyrim:Steamscorch Mine")** — A small [malachite](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite "Skyrim:Malachite") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in northeastern [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steamscorch+Mine)

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic Ruins

-  **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") north of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") led by [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ansilvund)
-  **[Hillgrund's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hillgrund%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Hillgrund's Tomb")** — A small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Hillgrund%27s+Tomb)
-  **[Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel")** — A small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Kagrenzel)
-  **[Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft")** — A large [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") south-southeast of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [Dwarven automatons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automatons "Skyrim:Dwarven Automatons"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mzulft)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Abandoned Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Prison "Skyrim:Abandoned Prison")** — A small [Imperial prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing the [ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") of its drowned prisoners. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Abandoned+Prison)
-  **[Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") initially occupied by [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Amol)
-  **[Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [Silver Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") and their leader [Krev the Skinner](/wiki/Skyrim:Krev_the_Skinner "Skyrim:Krev the Skinner"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gallows+Rock)
-  **[Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing") containing the [Mistwatch Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch_Bandit "Skyrim:Mistwatch Bandit") and their [leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Bandit Leader"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mistwatch)
-  **[Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and their leader [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Morvunskar)
-  **[Refugees' Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Refugees%27_Rest "Skyrim:Refugees' Rest")** — A small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") east of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Refugees%27+Rest)

### Standing Stones and Daedric Shrines

-  **[The Atronach Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Atronach_Stone "Skyrim:The Atronach Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stones "Skyrim:Standing Stones") scattered across Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Atronach+Stone)
-  **[Sacellum of Boethiah](/wiki/Skyrim:Sacellum_of_Boethiah "Skyrim:Sacellum of Boethiah")** — The [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sacellum+of+Boethiah)

### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

- **[Darkwater River](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_River "Skyrim:Darkwater River")** — A river connecting [Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir") to the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Darkwater+River)
- **[Dunmeth Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmeth_Pass "Skyrim:Dunmeth Pass")** — A mountain [pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Border_Gates "Skyrim:Border Gates") and one of the few traversable roads through the [Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Lore:Velothi_Mountains "Lore:Velothi Mountains") between northwest [Morrowind](/wiki/Lore:Morrowind "Lore:Morrowind") and northeast [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dunmeth+Pass)
-  **[Mara's Eye Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Mara%27s_Eye_Pond "Skyrim:Mara's Eye Pond")** — A small lake due east of [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Mara%27s+Eye+Pond)
- **[River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim")** — A river flowing from [Lake Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Yorgrim "Skyrim:Lake Yorgrim") to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=River+Yorgrim)
- **[Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts")** — A vast ocean to the north of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sea+of+Ghosts)
- **[Velothi Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Velothi_Mountains "Skyrim:Velothi Mountains")** — A mountain range that stretches along the eastern border of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Velothi+Mountains)
- **[White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River")** — The longest river in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)"), stretching from the south of the province to the northeast corner. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=White+River)
-  **[Witchmist Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Witchmist_Grove "Skyrim:Witchmist Grove")** — A small shack north of [Bonestrewn Crest](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonestrewn_Crest "Skyrim:Bonestrewn Crest") and south of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Witchmist+Grove)

### Unmarked Places

.jpg)

The dragon mound southwest of Kynesgrove, with Windhelm and Morvunskar visible in the background

- There are five [Dragon Mounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Mounds "Skyrim:Dragon Mounds") in Eastmarch.
  - East of [Kynesgrove](/wiki/Skyrim:Kynesgrove "Skyrim:Kynesgrove").
  - Southwest of Kynesgrove.
  - Northwest of [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill").
  - North of [Eldergleam Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Eldergleam_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Eldergleam Sanctuary").
  - West of [Mzulft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzulft "Skyrim:Mzulft").
- There are a few [Shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") in Eastmarch.
  - A [Shrine of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrine of Akatosh") northwest of [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern").
  - A [Shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrine of Dibella") west of [Abandoned Prison](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Prison "Skyrim:Abandoned Prison").
  - Two [Shrines of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines"):
    - Southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
    - East of [Cradlecrush Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradlecrush_Rock "Skyrim:Cradlecrush Rock").

## Eastmarch Quests

All the quests that are started in or are related to Eastmarch (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[A Blade in the Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Blade_in_the_Dark "Skyrim:A Blade in the Dark")**: Prove you are Dragonborn to [Delphine](/wiki/Skyrim:Delphine "Skyrim:Delphine") by slaying the dragon [Sahloknir](/wiki/Skyrim:Sahloknir "Skyrim:Sahloknir").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

### Imperial Legion Civil War Quests

- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol")**: Prepare for the final assault on [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") by taking [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm")**: Conquer the [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and bring [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") to justice!

### Stormcloaks Civil War Quests

- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Stormcloaks)")**: Find this [crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for Ulfric Stormcloak.
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Deliver an axe to the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun").
- **[Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")**: Take [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Daedric Quests

- **[Boethiah's Calling](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Calling "Skyrim:Boethiah's Calling")**: Become [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah")'s new champion.

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Innocence Lost](/wiki/Skyrim:Innocence_Lost "Skyrim:Innocence Lost")**: Help an orphaned [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") avoid being returned to a sadistic [caretaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind").
- **[Mourning Never Comes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mourning_Never_Comes "Skyrim:Mourning Never Comes")**: Help [Muiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Muiri "Skyrim:Muiri") get her revenge.
- **[Kill Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Kill Ma'randru-jo")**: Assassinate [Ma'randru-jo](/wiki/Skyrim:Ma%27randru-jo "Skyrim:Ma'randru-jo") to complete a [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") contract.

### College of Winterhold

- **[Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen")**: Learn the location of the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").

### Thieves Guild

- **[Summerset Shadows](/wiki/Skyrim:Summerset_Shadows "Skyrim:Summerset Shadows")**: Remove a rival guild from the picture.

### Companions

- **[The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand")**: Join the ranks of [the Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle") and clear [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") of werewolf hunters.

### Bards College

- **[Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute "Skyrim:Finn's Lute")**: Return an invaluable [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").

### Side Quests including Divine Quests

- **[The Blessings of Nature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Blessings_of_Nature "Skyrim:The Blessings of Nature")**: Restore the [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") for [Danica Pure-Spring](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring").
- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").
- **[Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial")**: Acquire the materials necessary to repair the [White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)").
- **[Rise in the East](/wiki/Skyrim:Rise_in_the_East "Skyrim:Rise in the East")**: Help the [East Empire Company](/wiki/Lore:East_Empire_Company "Lore:East Empire Company") take care of some [pirates](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_Horker "Skyrim:Blood Horker").

### Dawnguard Quests

- **[Lost to the Ages](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_to_the_Ages "Skyrim:Lost to the Ages")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Search for the Dwemer's [Aetherium Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Forge "Skyrim:The Aetherium Forge").

### Dragonborn Quests

- **[Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn"): Travel to the island of [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") to find out what's happening there.

### Creation Club Quests

- **[Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put a stop to two bandit gangs wielding strange otherworldly equipment.
- **[The Edge of Ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Edge_of_Ruin "Skyrim:The Edge of Ruin")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge"): Find a madwoman's [legendary bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruin%27s_Edge_(item) "Skyrim:Ruin's Edge (item)").
- **[Heart of Crimson](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_of_Crimson "Skyrim:Heart of Crimson")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Ebony_Plate "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Ebony Plate"): Confront the murderous leader of a bandit gang.
- **[Missing Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_Merchant "Skyrim:Missing Merchant")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail"): A powerful set of armor has come on the market.
- **[Pets of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim_(quest) "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Pets_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Pets of Skyrim"): Find trained pets around Skyrim.
- **[Through a Glass, Darkly](/wiki/Skyrim:Through_a_Glass,_Darkly "Skyrim:Through a Glass, Darkly")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend "Skyrim:Shadowrend"): Confront the darkness within yourself to obtain a [powerful weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowrend_(item) "Skyrim:Shadowrend (item)").
- **[Tilted Scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Tilted_Scales "Skyrim:Tilted Scales")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Dragonscale "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Dragonscale"): Retrieve a set of ancient armor from an old warrior.

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests, such as favors, are located in Eastmarch. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Eastmarch "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

## Notes

- Eastmarch also [appears](/wiki/Online:Eastmarch "Online:Eastmarch") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") is in the [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") crime faction, rather than the Eastmarch one.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.
- Oddly, since the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") is marked as being owned by the Winterhold crime faction, if you help anyone in the hold (including [Kjar](/wiki/Skyrim:Kjar "Skyrim:Kjar") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and ironically enough, anyone from the [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)")), you will be able to take things from the longhouse without it being considered theft.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19319)) A new faction was created specifically for the residents of the longhouse in order to set ownership correctly.
